# the Metascience Project Labbook -- joint Claude Science <-> Claude Code research log

<!-- WHAT THIS FILE IS: the append-only joint labbook. Every unit of work by Claude Science [CS], the assistant [the assistant], or a blank Claude Code [CC] is
     logged here. It is the TOP documentation duty and the reproducibility backbone of the submission.
     HOW TO USE: append ONE entry per work unit using the schema below. NEVER edit or delete a past entry; a
     correction is a NEW entry that references the old LB-NNN. Write in ENGLISH. Timestamps in CEST. Append
     LINUX-NATIVE (atomic) to avoid write races; read freely via the Windows symlink. Newest entry at the bottom. -->

## Rules
- **Append-only.** Never edit/delete a past entry. Correction = a new entry referencing the old `LB-NNN`.
- **English only.** Timestamps in **CEST** (the operator's zone). Tags: `[CS]` = Claude Science, `[the assistant]` = the assistant (Mission-Control), `[CC]` = a blank Claude Code executor.
- **One entry per work unit** (task / experiment step / run / decision).
- **Cite sources by number** from `SOURCES.md`, each with a short what/why.

## Schema
```
### LB-NNN | YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM CEST | [CS|the assistant|CC] | <short clear header>
- **Goal:** <idea / aim of the task or experiment>
- **What & how:** <what was done, how carried out - method, tools, CS session ref or run-NNN>
- **Outcome:** <the exact result - numbers, finding, pass/fail, decision>
- **Data / artifacts:** <where it lives + exact filenames>
- **Sources:** <S-NNN (short what/why it was used), ...>
```

---
<!-- ENTRIES BELOW (append-only, newest at the bottom) -->

### LB-014 | 2026-07-09 09:40 CEST | [CS] | Literature grounding of the eval methodology + test-set v1 drafted (aging/metabolism/mito)
- **Goal:** Before designing, do real literature research on how to measure "better" and "novel" scientifically (operator instruction: work scientifically, use established methodology), and stand up the test set on the operator's domain.
- **What & how:** Searched OpenAlex (via injected API key, from the analysis kernel — repl path is proxy-blocked for OpenAlex) across 6 methodology topics; pulled abstracts of the load-bearing papers; probed the aging prior-art landscape via the live PubMed connector. Registered S-006..S-012. Wrote `loop-design/current/method-foundations.md` (the cited basis for every measurement choice). Created `test-sets/2026-07-09_testset_aging-v1/` with 4 tiered seed questions (design principles: open hypothesis-generation, word-identical, has a prior-art baseline for literature-distance novelty, rewards exploiting many CS connectors) + a concrete idiot-safe `request-to-operator.md`.
- **Outcome — adopted methods (all cited):** (A) eval design = blinded, confounder-controlled, head-to-head, normalized template so judges are blind to arm (Si/Yang/Hashimoto S-006; their finding "AI more novel, slightly less feasible" grounds novelty×plausibility + sets realistic expectations). (B) scalable scoring = LLM-as-judge with chain-of-thought + form-filling (G-Eval S-007), with judge-bias controls + a multi-judge PANEL incl. a non-Claude judge (Codex) + pairwise Elo for drift-robust ranking (MT-Bench/Arena S-008). (C) creativity = novelty × usefulness/plausibility (meta-theory S-009); novelty = distance from prior art / atypical combination (science-of-science S-010) computed as inverse semantic similarity to nearest OpenAlex/PubMed work; aging domain has a dense baseline (S-011: hallmarks 8,596 / mito 3,951 / senolytics 1,101 / exercise-mimetic 87). (D) outer loop = Meta-Harness outer loop (S-005) with one-variable-per-experiment DoE + ≥2 runs+mean. Test-set: 4 draft questions Q1-Q4 (T1-T3), awaiting the operator confirm (non-blocking — I proceed on seeds; he can adjust).
- **Data / artifacts:** `loop-design/current/method-foundations.md`; `test-sets/2026-07-09_testset_aging-v1/{README.md, request-to-operator.md}`; `SOURCES.md` S-006..S-012.
- **Sources:** S-006 (blinded AI-idea eval), S-007 (G-Eval judge), S-008 (LLM-judge bias/Elo), S-009 (creativity=novelty×usefulness), S-010 (novelty as distance/atypicality), S-011 (aging prior-art baseline via PubMed), S-012 (OpenAlex methodology search).

### LB-015 | 2026-07-09 10:05 CEST | [CS] | D1 written: the Experiment-Loop design doc + two-loop schematic
- **Goal:** Produce D1 — the experimental design that makes the whole project a controlled experiment: how CS runs the outer loop, the arms, the controls, the test/baseline strategy, the improvement-category search space, and the threats to validity. Grounded in the method foundations (LB-014).
- **What & how:** Wrote `loop-design/current/experiment-loop-design.md` (v0). Key design decisions recorded: (1) the outer loop is a Meta-Harness outer loop (S-005) searching Agentic-Loop designs; (2) roles + the LOCKED isolation boundary (blank CC never touches the repo; the assistant alone bridges outputs back); (3) DoE discipline — one manipulated variable per experiment (= improvement category), fixed controls, no memory/drift, ≥2 runs+mean; (4) two arms answering word-identical questions, outputs normalized+blinded before scoring (S-006, S-008); (5) **test/baseline strategy = hybrid**: primary = constant tests vs a fixed baseline (clean improvement curve, cheaper/lower-variance), secondary = one end-of-run escalation to a harder tier with baseline re-drawn (tests "stronger loop widens the gap"); reasoning: moving test+baseline every round confounds "loop better" with "test harder"; (6) the improvement-category search space C1-C6 ranked by benefit÷cost (context prompt, Specialists, connector-depth, Codex panel, CC sub-agent panel [RAM-gated], recombination); (7) autonomy = pre-clear CS permission scopes + a watchdog sub-agent, graceful degrade to human-relayed approval; (8) threats to validity named (self-enhancement bias, novelty≠correctness, small n, drive variance, overfitting → final question chosen later by the operator, distinct from test set). Built the two-loop schematic (`experiment_loop.png`) with figure-style; §9.1 geometric check = 0 text overlaps.
- **Outcome:** D1 done (v0). Establishes the measurable, controlled experiment; feeds quantification.md + creativity-metric.md (the metrics) next.
- **Data / artifacts:** `loop-design/current/experiment-loop-design.md`, `loop-design/current/experiment_loop.png`.
- **Sources:** S-002 (ERA tree-search/idea-injection), S-003 (Robin replication/variance), S-004 (Co-Scientist arms+Elo+expert), S-005 (Meta-Harness outer loop, harness>model), S-006 (blinded head-to-head + confounder control), S-008 (judge bias controls + Elo).

### LB-016 | 2026-07-09 10:25 CEST | [CS] | Quantification methods defined: 5-dim rubric + auto checks + judge panel
- **Goal:** Define the fixed, blinded, multi-dimensional metric that makes "better" measurable identically across arms + iterations — the yardstick D2 is built on.
- **What & how:** Wrote `loop-design/current/quantification.md` (v1) + machine-readable `rubric.json` (validated: 5 dims, weights sum to 1.0) + a scorecard mock figure (`scorecard_mock.png`, labeled illustrative). The metric: 5 anchored 1-5 dimensions — Grounding 0.25, Correctness 0.25, Completeness 0.20, Usefulness 0.15, Creativity 0.15 (weights guard feasibility per S-006's "AI novelty outruns feasibility" finding; sensitivity-checked in analysis). Judges fill a form per dimension {score, 1-sentence justification, evidence_span} = G-Eval form-filling (S-007). Automatic checks (run every iteration, cheap, auditable): (2a) CITATION VERIFICATION — extract every citation → resolve existence via PubMed/OpenAlex → LLM entailment check that the cited source actually supports the claim → rate caps Grounding (the credibility/hallucination backbone); (2b) entity-specificity count → Completeness; (2c) plausibility red-flags (seeded by the operator's calibration answer) → Creativity's plausibility gate. Judge PANEL (S-008): ≥2 judges incl. a non-Claude judge (Codex) to blunt self-enhancement bias; randomize arm order; blind style; report inter-judge agreement + judge-vs-the operator agreement (weighted κ); plus a pairwise Elo cross-check. Primary endpoint = Δweighted-composite (Arm L − Arm B) vs run-to-run spread. Honesty guards recorded (never composite-alone, never novelty without plausibility gate, alternate-weighting sensitivity).
- **Outcome:** Quantification done (v1). rubric.json is the harness's loadable contract. Creativity dim (5) detailed next in creativity-metric.md.
- **Data / artifacts:** `loop-design/current/{quantification.md, rubric.json, scorecard_mock.png}`.
- **Sources:** S-006 (blinded, feasibility guard), S-007 (G-Eval form-filling judge), S-008 (panel + bias controls + Elo), S-009 (creativity=novelty×usefulness), S-011 (connectors for citation verification).

### LB-018 | 2026-07-09 11:10 CEST | [CS] | Creativity/novelty metric designed + REAL worked example (the GOAL's open question)
- **Goal:** Answer the GOAL's explicit open question — measure genuine novelty/creativity while breaking the "AI recombines old stuff" bias AND the operator's added requirement: a reasonability/reasoning check is essential or novelty is just hallucination; "a clear understandable creative line of thought has to be behind creative breakthroughs."
- **What & how:** Wrote `loop-design/current/creativity-metric.md` (v1). Definition: creativity_index = Novelty × Plausibility_gate × ReasoningTrace_gate — a MULTIPLICATIVE product (any one factor near zero kills the score), grounding creativity=novelty×usefulness (S-009) + novelty=distance-from-prior-art (S-010) + the operator's reasoning-trace gate as the anti-hallucination core. Novelty = retrieval-frequency 1/(1+log10(1+hits)) primary + semantic distance (flagged model-dependent). Plausibility gate = red-flag checklist (the operator-seeded) → (P-1)/4. Reasoning-trace gate = judge scores legibility of the derivation R∈1..5 and MUST quote the reasoning chain (R=5 explicit premises→mechanism→falsifiable prediction+distinguishing control; R=1 bare assertion = hallucination signature) → (R-1)/4; a novel hypothesis with R≤2 is treated as candidate hallucination and cannot score creative.
- **Worked example (REAL, live July-2026 PubMed prior-art + host.llm panel):** 4 aging hypotheses. H1 textbook (2873 hits, N=0.22, R=5) → index 0.168; H2 derivative (13 hits, N=0.47, R=4) → 0.262; H3 novel-but-thin (0 hits, N=1.00, R=2) → **0.125 (LOWEST)**; H3+ SAME novel idea but explicitly derived (0 hits, N=1.00, R=4) → **0.375 (HIGHEST)**. KEY RESULT: H3 and H3+ have identical maximal novelty + identical plausibility and differ ONLY in reasoning legibility, yet score 3× apart — the operator's principle quantified. Also found: naive TF-IDF lexical cosine barely discriminates novelty (all 0.84-0.93) because domain vocab is shared → metric leans on retrieval-frequency, not lexical distance (honest caveat recorded). Elo pairwise cross-check specified for drift-robust ranking (S-004, S-008).
- **Data / artifacts:** `loop-design/current/creativity-metric.md` + `creativity_worked_example.png`; provenance in `cs-artifacts/phase-1_experiment-loop-design/`: `2026-07-09_1030_result_creativity-priorart-neighbors.json` (real PubMed neighbours), `..._creativity-reasoning-assessment.json` (real panel scores), `..._creativity-worked-scores.json` (composite indices), `..._artifact_creativity-worked-example.png`. Manifest + SOURCES updated.
- **Sources:** S-006 (novelty needs feasibility guard), S-009 (creativity=novelty×usefulness), S-010 (novelty=distance/atypicality), S-011 (PubMed prior-art), S-004/S-008 (Elo cross-check).

### LB-019 | 2026-07-09 11:40 CEST | [CS] | Operator prior-experience input (A–G) captured → reshapes the loop to Mission-Control architecture
- **Goal:** Per the operator instruction (ask for prior-experience input BEFORE authoring the blank-CC Agentic-Loop setup), I asked; the operator handed over 7 findings from real prior CC-drives-CS runs. Capture them (labbook = source of truth) + record CS's design response to each, before building the v0 loop.
- **What & how:** Wrote `loop-design/current/operator-design-input.md` (findings A–G verbatim-in-substance + CS response each). Registered S-014. Summary + how it changes the design:
  - **A [central] Context window is binding** — a single flat CC driver runs out of context (even 1M) from constant CS polling + subagent panels. Fix: **Mission-Control architecture** — start CC splits task into substeps + acts as MC; a FRESH CC session runs the CS loop per substep, reports back, MC launches next, then a CS session integrates all substeps. Automated relay preferred over human copy-paste. Watch `claude -p` budget. → v0 loop becomes hierarchical orchestrator–worker (= Co-Scientist Supervisor+worker S-004; context-isolation S-005).
  - **B [central] Poll cadence** — polling every ~1 min wasted context; **~5 min better, best ~10 min + grant all permissions ONCE project-wide up front.** → watchdog poll ≥5 min (default 10) + pre-flight project-wide permission grant.
  - **C [central, open] Multi-session-in-one-project** — substep CS sessions in the SAME new CS project (fresh project per loop-build); need to work out cross-session data sharing. → CS response: sessions share artifact store + project memory + host.query; coordinate via artifacts + a shared handoff manifest; VERIFY in dry-run.
  - **D [insight] Review loop after the PLAN** — a gate after plan + after results; especially after the plan you can inject creativity/ambition, much cheaper than re-running results. → two review gates: plan-stage (creativity injection, cheap, default-on) + results-stage (correctness, budget-gated).
  - **E [insight] Panel design** — correctness-obsessed checker FIRST (verify every quote/dataset/code = anti-hallucination), THEN a 2-lens × 2-brain panel: identical instructions on Opus 4.8 AND Codex/GPT-5.5; lenses = ambitious young postdoc (dream big, push to Nature) vs experienced mentoring PI (reliable/lean methodology, controls, bulletproof story, anti over-engineering); productive tension; comparator + chairman synthesis (Karpathy council); "must be done well." → loop's internal improvement engine, gate-first ordering, 2×2 blunts self-enhancement bias (S-008).
  - **F [central principle] KEEP WHAT IS GOOD** — protect solid results first; don't drift into hallucination/over-engineering; always "what is good + why FIRST, then improve with evidence + reasoning." → mandatory KEEP pass opening every review gate; every IMPROVE needs evidence+reasoning.
  - **G [central] Web + literature access for ALL CC sessions/subagents** + enforce citations/CoT → lower hallucination. → full connector suite + citation-verification enforced (ties to quantification Grounding + creativity reasoning-trace).
  - Operator framing: A/B/C/G are central flags; D/E/F are validated-but-improvable first insights — "MUCH more to discover and improve, that is your task; test against a bulletproof, judge-convincing quantification + rating system."
- **Outcome:** Loop design upgraded from flat "CC drives CS" to a Mission-Control orchestrator with two review gates + a KEEP-first correctness→2×2-panel→comparator→chairman improvement engine, ≥5-10 min cadence, project-wide permissions, literature-grounded + citation-enforced. Feeds the v0 loop (step 6) + updates the improvement-category search space in D1.
- **Data / artifacts:** `loop-design/current/operator-design-input.md`; SOURCES S-014.
- **Sources:** S-014 (the findings), S-004 (Supervisor+worker), S-005 (context isolation/Meta-Harness), S-008 (2-brain panel vs self-enhancement bias).

### LB-020 | 2026-07-09 12:05 CEST | [CS] | Scoring harness built + dry-run-verified + real-connector smoke-tested (the runnable core of the quantification)
- **Goal:** Turn the quantification (rubric.json) + creativity-metric.md into a REAL, runnable, dry-run-verifiable scoring harness — the machine that scores Arm B (baseline) vs Arm L (loop) answers. Must run OFFLINE (deterministic, for CI/crash-recovery) AND against live host.llm + host.mcp connectors in a real CS session.
- **Design decisions (why it is shaped this way):**
  1. **Dependency injection** — the scoring core (extract/novelty/citations/judge/composite/elo) is PURE (no host.* imports); all LLM + connector calls are injected via an adapters layer. Two adapter sets: `DryRunAdapters` (offline deterministic stubs) and `RealAdapters(host, codex_fn, reasoning_model)` (wraps host.llm Claude judge + a Codex judge + host.mcp PubMed/OpenAlex). This makes the harness testable without network and portable into a CS session unchanged.
  2. **Grounding is capped by citation verification** (quantification.md §2a): every citation is (i) resolved for existence, (ii) checked for ENTAILMENT (does the cited abstract actually support the claim?). verification_rate → a hard MAX on the Grounding dimension. No citations at all → cap 2. This is the credibility backbone.
  3. **Creativity is the multiplicative gate** (creativity-metric.md §1): creativity_index = novelty × plausibility_gate × reasoning_trace_gate, overriding the judges' free-text creativity score. Novelty = 0.75·retrieval-frequency + 0.25·semantic-distance (retrieval-frequency primary because TF-IDF under-discriminates, LB-018).
  4. **Judge panel = ≥2 judges incl. a non-Claude (Codex)** (S-008) with G-Eval form-filling (S-007) + inter-judge agreement tracked. The creativity judge MUST quote the reasoning chain (anti-hallucination).
  5. **Elo tournament** (elo.py) for drift-robust relative ranking across arms/iterations (S-004, S-008), position-order randomized.
  6. **Defense-in-depth:** citation cap, entity-specificity, reasoning-trace gate, and hallucination_flag are INDEPENDENT guards — a bad answer must beat all of them, not one.
- **Dry-run verification (offline, deterministic — `test_dryrun.py`):** 13/13 checks PASS. Fixture = 1 aging question, Arm B ×2 (vague, uncited) + Arm L ×3 (two good cited+reasoned, one TRAP with fabricated PMID 00000001 + fake DOI + no reasoning). Verified behaviours + EXACT composites (from scorecard.csv): (a) fabricated citations → verification_rate 0.0 → grounding_cap 1 → the trap gets the LOWEST composite of all five (1.81, below the weak baselines B=2.06); (b) real citations verify 1.0 → grounding_cap 5; (c) loop beats baseline — the two GOOD loop answers = 3.37/3.32 vs B=2.06, so **good-vs-baseline Δ=+1.28**; the whole Arm-L mean INCLUDING the trap = 2.83, so **arm-level Δ=+0.77** (the harness reports the arm-level delta; the gap between +1.28 and +0.77 is exactly the trap being dragged down, i.e. the machinery working); (d) Elo ranks the trap LAST, below both baselines (L#1 1083 > L#2 1043 > B 958 > L#3-trap 957); (e) weights sum to 1.0; (f) scorecard.json + scorecard.csv emitted.
- **Real-connector smoke test (live host.mcp PubMed):** search_articles + get_article_metadata paths both return live data (query→total_count+pmids; pmids→title+abstract). IMPORTANT FINDING: the "fake" PMID 00000001 resolved to a NON-EMPTY article record (count=1) rather than nothing — i.e. a fabricated/mistyped low-value PMID can still resolve to *an* article, so an existence check ALONE is insufficient. This VALIDATES the two-stage citation design: the ENTAILMENT stage (claim vs cited abstract) is the real guard against misattributed-but-real citations, not existence. Real-mode resolver returns the title+abstract so entailment + human audit can catch mismatches. (No code change needed — the design already handles it; noted as a real-mode caveat in the harness README.)
- **Data / artifacts (all generated 2026-07-09 ~11:45–12:05 CEST, in `experiments/exp-001_baseline-vs-v0-loop/01_setup/workspace/harness/`):** `scoring/__init__.py`, `scoring/extract.py` (citations + checkable entities), `scoring/novelty.py`, `scoring/citations.py`, `scoring/judge.py`, `scoring/composite.py`, `scoring/elo.py`, `adapters.py` (DryRun + Real), `run_scoring.py` (orchestrator/CLI), `test_dryrun.py` (12 asserts), `answers.example.json` (fixture), `rubric.json` (copy of the canonical), plus `out/scorecard.{json,csv}` (dry-run output). exp-001 folder scaffolded from _TEMPLATE.
- **Sources:** S-007 (G-Eval form-filling), S-008 (LLM-judge biases, 2-brain panel, Elo), S-004 (Elo tournament / Supervisor), S-010 (novelty=distance), rubric.json (S-013 folder), creativity-metric.md (LB-018).

### LB-021 | 2026-07-09 12:20 CEST | [CS] | DECISION: v0 Agentic Loop = FLAT single-session loop; Mission-Control deferred to a measurable improvement category
- **Goal:** Decide the architecture of the v0 Agentic Loop before authoring it (operator was asked; see the two options below).
- **Decision (operator):** Start v0 as a **simple flat single-session loop** (one blank CC drives one CS session through plan→act→review→integrate), NOT the Mission-Control orchestrator. Introduce **Mission-Control as improvement category C1** in a later iteration, measured against this flat v0 baseline.
- **Provenance of this decision:** CS presented the choice via a structured `ask_user` prompt ("v0 loop architecture") offering (a) proceed with Mission-Control v0, (b) simplify v0 + add MC later, (c) operator adds notes first. The operator selected option (b) "**Simplify v0, add MC later — Start with a single-session flat loop for exp-001; introduce Mission-Control as a tested improvement category in a later iteration.**" This entry records that selection; the scientific rationale below is CS's, endorsed by the operator's choice.
- **Why this is the right call (scientific):** It makes the context-window fix (operator finding A) an EARNED, quantified result rather than a baked-in assumption. D2's whole job is "which improvement category helps most, and by how much" — so the Mission-Control benefit must be measured as Δcomposite vs a simpler baseline, not assumed. A flat v0 is also the cleanest possible first baseline (fewer moving parts → less to debug on the first real run) and de-risks exp-001. Operator framing (S-014) explicitly called A/B/C/G central flags but D/E/F "first insights to improve" — this keeps the loop honestly improvable.
- **What still goes INTO v0 (the cheap, always-on findings):** finding B (poll cadence ≥5 min, default 10 + project-wide permission pre-grant), finding G (full connector suite + citation enforcement), finding D (a plan-stage review pass — cheap creativity/ambition injection), finding F (KEEP-what-is-good opens every review). Deferred to later categories: finding A/C (Mission-Control multi-session = C1), finding E (2-lens×2-brain panel = C3).
- **Outcome:** v0 loop spec to be authored flat with B/D/F/G built in; C1 (Mission-Control) + C3 (2×2 panel) are the first improvement categories exp-002+ will test. D1 §7 already lists these as C1/C3.

- **Goal:** Author the v0 Agentic Loop (the inner product, GOAL D3) as a flat single-session loop (per LB-021), and instantiate it as the first experiment exp-001 (baseline vs v0-loop) with a self-contained setup a blank Claude Code can run in isolation.
- **What & how:**

Scope honesty: n=1 question × ≥2 runs = proof-of-instrument + first signal, not a powered study.

  5. **`01_setup/protocol.md`** — defines BOTH arms: Arm B (raw CS, one message, cold, FRESH session) and Arm L (v0 loop, separate fresh session); byte-identical question wording is the core fairness rule; run order B-first; run_log duties; RUN_REPORT.md format (header/ArmB/ArmL/fairness attestation/anomalies/files); explains the scoring contract so the CC understands what CS does after.

### LB-023 | 2026-07-09 12:55 CEST | [CS] | the assistant-facing specs + the operator human-eval instruments authored (exp-001 01_setup/for-the operator/)
- **Goal:** Author the instruments that turn a raw run into analysable data: how the assistant (Mission-Control) reports to CS, and how the operator (human expert anchor) evaluates — GOAL success dimension 5 (human eval) + the anchor that validates/recalibrates the harness.
- **What & how:**
  1. **`for-the operator/eval-sheet-template.md`** — the operator's standardized blinded eval sheet. Part A: score EACH of the two (blinded, order-randomized) answers 1–5 on the SAME 5 rubric dimensions the harness uses (so machine-vs-human agreement is computable). Part B: the creativity honesty check (is the novel idea actually novel? can you follow the reasoning chain? flag if asserted = possible hallucination) — directly operationalizes the reasoning-trace gate. Part C: blinded head-to-head + confidence. Part D: the AI-slop red-flag detector (wrong-direction/dose/contraindication/mechanism-contradiction/correlation-as-causation/misused-citation) → seeds the harness plausibility gate. Part E: free comment. the operator is the anchor; on disagreement the operator overrides the harness.
  2. **`for-the operator/final-report-spec.md`** — the contract for the assistant's `03_final-report.md`: run summary + fairness attestation; harness scores table (per-arm/run 5 dims + composite + creativity_index + citation-verify-rate, Δcomposite vs pooled SD, Elo, RAW scorecard.json/csv attached); a mandatory anti-hallucination audit (every flagged/unsupported citation listed); the operator's verbatim eval + a the operator-vs-harness agreement table; a machine-readable JSON summary block CS parses; neutral observations only (the assistant does NOT recommend the next loop — that's CS, and does NOT judge the science — that's the operator).
  3. **`for-the operator/present-to-operator-skill.md`** — spec for the CC skill the assistant runs to present exp-001 to the operator: blind + randomize (true mapping in an the assistant-only `_blinding_key.md`, never shown to the operator), present understandably, take the operator's questions WITHOUT coaching, capture scores verbatim into `04_evaluation.md`, unblind only after saving. Hard bias-control rules: blinding sacred, no leading, verbatim capture, the operator is the anchor.
- **Design principle:** the three roles are kept clean — the assistant measures + reports (no science judgment, no loop design), the operator judges the science (blinded, anchor), CS designs + analyses. Blinding + order-randomization + verbatim capture protect the human-eval result from bias.
- **Data / artifacts (2026-07-09 ~12:50–12:55 CEST):** `experiments/exp-001_baseline-vs-v0-loop/01_setup/for-the operator/{eval-sheet-template.md, final-report-spec.md, present-to-operator-skill.md}`.

That consultation is the immediate next step; this entry records the CS-drafted v1 that the operator's input will refine.
- **Sources:** S-004 (Co-Scientist blinded expert novelty/impact rubric — direct prior art for the human eval), S-008 (blinding + bias controls in LLM/human evaluation), S-006 (blinded head-to-head expert eval), creativity-metric.md (Part B/D feed the gates).

### LB-024 | 2026-07-09 13:20 CEST | [CS] | Operator eval-design consultation (part 1): execution model + test count + question set + budget reasoning
- **Goal:** Operator asked to be consulted as human-expert-in-the-loop, before locking the eval instruments, on (i) tests per setup, (ii) results presentation, (iii) eval categories that matter. This entry logs the decisions from part 1 (i + adjacent execution-model + budget questions). Parts (ii)+(iii) are the next consultation step (still open).
- **Decisions (operator, via structured asks):**
  1. **Tests per setup = 2 questions × 2 runs/arm** (operator picked option 2 of 4). 8 answers total per setup (2 Q × [2 Arm-B runs + 2 Arm-L runs]). Rationale: guards against a one-question fluke while staying light on eval-time + CC budget.
  2. **Question set = Q1 + Q3** (CS recommendation, operator did not override). Q1 (T1, mitophagy→sarcopenia, moderate prior-art density ~3,951) + Q3 (T2, approved-drug exercise-mimetic repurposing, SPARSE prior-art ~87 → high novelty headroom). Chosen to span the novelty-density spectrum, both in the operator's core expertise (authoritative human eval), and to exercise different connector sets (Q1: PubMed/OpenTargets/Reactome/GTEx; Q3: +ChEMBL/openFDA/ClinicalTrials). Q2 (crowded NAD+, overlaps Q1) and Q4 (T3 multi-hallmark, very open) deferred to a later, more mature iteration.
  3. **v0 execution model = AUTONOMOUS blank-CC** (operator picked "Keep autonomous CC v0"). CS proposed an alternative interactive human-in-the-loop model (operator drives one CC session, approves cards) to cut CC-budget + solve permission cards for free; operator DECLINED it and chose to keep the self-driving headless bootstrap as authored (LB-022). Consequence: `bootstrap.md`/`protocol.md` stay autonomous (no rewrite); the always-on throttles from finding B (poll ≥5 min/default 10 + one-time project-wide permission pre-grant) remain the budget guard. The interactive model is retained as a possible later comparison, not v0.
- **Budget reasoning recorded (corrected for accuracy):** Two SEPARATE budget pools, and it is AUTHENTICATION, not interactive-vs-headless mode, that picks the pool. **Pool A = the OAuth subscription allowance** (used by Claude Code in BOTH interactive and `claude -p` headless mode) — this is what the CC uses now (pre-check §E: API key ABSENT, only OAuth). **Pool B = the $200 Console API credits** — used ONLY if an API key is wired into Claude Code; currently IDLE/unusable (pre-check §E17). Wiring the $200 key would let `claude -p` + the Agent SDK bill against Pool B instead of the subscription, decoupling runs from subscription rate limits (the thing that can stall a run) — substantial but finite (Opus-class is the priciest tier; ~a handful of large runs; exact rate = check Console). CORRECTION vs an earlier in-chat statement: the pre-check rates the plan tier as UNKNOWN (not confirmed Max) and says nothing about allowance reset mechanics — I over-stated "rolling window / weekly cap"; not sourced. Where CC budget is spent: Arm B ≈ 1 CC touch/answer (negligible); Arm L ≈ 6 CC→CS exchanges/run + polling (≈85% of CC spend). - **Goal:** Operator sharpened the experimental control. Integrate + lock the definitive fairness model and fix a latent flaw in the earlier loop draft.

Baseline gets the bare naive question; only the loop reframes.

So the CC start package IS `01_setup/workspace/`, and `workspace/CLAUDE.md` is its operating manual: identity + the fairness rule + ground rules (isolation, cadence, budget, honesty) + the full runnable loop (STEP 0 REFRAME → FRAME → PLAN → PLAN-REVIEW → ACT → RESULT-REVIEW → INTEGRATE). QUALITY = venue + primary-vs-review + retraction NEW module); 5B provenance verification (did steps really happen, ✓ badges); 5C the 5-dim rubric (grounding .25/correctness .25/completeness .20/usefulness .15/creativity .15) via blinded ≥2-judge G-Eval panel incl. a non-Claude model; 5D creativity index = Novelty(retrieval-freq) × Plausibility_gate × ReasoningTrace_gate (multiplicative; no reasoning trace on a novel claim → scored as candidate hallucination); 5E Elo + primary endpoint (Δcomposite vs pooled run-to-run SD, success = Δ>SD across both questions); 5F the the operator↔CS split (the operator = science only per answer; CS = all citations/provenance/composite; the operator is the human ground-truth CS checks its instrument against; both are submission data; final populated eval site ships in submission).

### LB-031 | 2026-07-09 16:05 CEST | [CS] | Operator proposed a major simplification (drop the assistant from the critical path; CS owns capture→score→eval-prep→report→next) + 4 scoring questions; CS analysis + proposed changes (PENDING operator GO)
- **Goal:** Operator asked 3 workflow questions + proposed a simpler architecture + asked 4 questions about what CS evaluates. Capture the input, analyze, propose changes. NOTHING built — awaiting GO (both on this AND on HTML v2).

The run-bundle is a **container built AROUND the raw answer by whoever captures it**, applied identically to both arms. CS just answers naturally; the loop naturally elicits more (citations/figures/reasoning) because that IS the treatment (finding G); the capture convention (answer.md + figures/ + process_trace + citations) is neutral and identical for both arms. The richness difference is the measured effect, not a format imposed on one arm. → keeps fairness intact.

CS agrees with operator that under the proposed simplification this is **largely redundant** with CS's own scoring report.

Operator is the A→B bridge (copies start-prompts, bootstrap workspaces, output folders, eval results) under CS instruction. **the assistant only if the blank CC/loop CRASHES** (blackbox forensic report). CS can make skills/protocols for this workflow.

If yes → the operator fills it in the CS tab + pastes JSON to chat (cleanest). If only static render → open the HTML in a browser tab; copy→paste capture works either way. Do NOT overclaim interactivity until tested.
- **Q4a — citations: independent agent? quantifiable/plottable?** CS: YES — a DEDICATED citation-scoring agent (separate host.llm call + own system prompt, isolated from the rubric judges so grounding isn't contaminated by overall impression). Quantifiable metrics per answer, all plottable at submission: n_citations; existence_rate (% resolve to real papers); support_rate (% where cited paper entails the claim, via entailment); primary_vs_review_ratio; venue_quality distribution; retraction_count; composite grounding 0–1. → bar charts per arm.
- **Q4b — rubric: can CS spawn a non-Claude model?** **CHECKED host.list_models() = Claude-family ONLY** (claude-sonnet-5, claude-opus-4-8, …); current=claude-opus-4-8, reasoning=claude-sonnet-5. **No GPT/Codex from the CS scoring kernel.** Operator's assumption CONFIRMED: CS's judge panel is realistically **2× Claude with DIFFERENT LENSES/system-prompts** (e.g. ambitious-young-postdoc vs mentoring-PI, operator finding E), varied temperature/seed — NOT cross-vendor. **CORRECTION:** earlier specs (quantification.md, dataflow-and-handoffs.md §5C) said "a non-Claude model e.g. Codex/GPT" for the CS panel — that is FALSE on the CS side + must be fixed. A genuine non-Claude judge exists ONLY on the CC side (codex MCP) → possible as a future improvement category (relay a Codex score back), not in CS's own harness. Bias control = different lenses + anchored rubric + inter-judge agreement, honestly labeled within-vendor.
- **Q4c — creativity index: computable? quantifiable/scientific?** YES — already computed in the worked example (LB-018): creativity = Novelty × Plausibility_gate × ReasoningTrace_gate. Novelty = OBJECTIVE retrieval frequency (real PubMed/OpenAlex hit counts → 1/(1+log10(1+hits))); the two gates = anchored LLM ratings (1–5) normalized. Product → 0–1, plottable. Demonstrated discrimination: H3 vs H3+ (same novel idea, reasoning legibility only) scored 3× apart. To make it MORE scientific: the novelty term is fully reproducible; anchor the gate rubrics + multi-rater agreement + report the components separately so a reviewer can audit each.
- **Q4d — what is an Elo cross-check?** The chess rating system applied to answers: judges make BLINDED pairwise comparisons ("is X better than Y?") across all answers for a question; win/loss → an Elo rating per answer; the arm ranking higher wins. It's a SECOND, independent read on loop-vs-baseline that does NOT depend on the absolute 1–5 composite — robust because pairwise preference is more stable across sessions than absolute scoring. If composite AND Elo agree → finding is solid; if they disagree → flag. Prior art: Co-Scientist tournament (S-004).
- **PROPOSED CHANGES pending GO (none built yet):** (1) adopt operator's simplified flow → rewrite dataflow-and-handoffs.md (CS owns capture→score→eval-prep→report→next; operator=bridge; the assistant=crash-only), update DOCUMENTATION §4/§4b + roles, repurpose the for-the operator/ specs to for-operator/ or fold into CS protocol; (2) fix the non-Claude-model overclaim in quantification.md + dataflow §5C → "2× Claude different lenses"; (3) build a citation-scoring agent + quantifiable citation metrics; (4) keep creativity index as-is, add component-level reporting; (5) author a CS-side skill/protocol for the run→score→report loop; (6) HTML v2 per LB-029, gated on the SAME GO.

### LB-036 | 2026-07-09 18:10 CEST | [CS] | Eval-site REDESIGN — operator rejected the retro-futuristic dark theme; rebuilt light/warm/low-fatigue (DEMO v3). SUPERSEDES the LB-029 point-8 aesthetic.

- **Research (quick, grounded):** UX/eye-strain sources converge: (1) avoid pure white AND pure black — use a soft warm off-white/cream background with deep-charcoal (not black) text to cut glare while keeping contrast; (2) warm palettes feel more comfortable and keep users on-page longer; (3) but keep contrast solid — low-contrast text is a top cause of eye fatigue; (4) muted accents used sparingly, not bright/saturated in large doses.
- **Redesign (CSS-only; HTML structure + JS + all field wiring untouched — same class names):** palette = cream page #f6f1e7, soft-white cards #fffdf8, deep warm-charcoal text #2f2a24, muted teal accent #2e8b83, warm ochre question headers #b9772e, muted green/brick semantic badges. REMOVED: CRT scanline overlay, grid backdrop, neon glow/text-shadows, all-caps letter-spaced headers, dark chrome.

### LB-042 | 2026-07-09 21:20 CEST | [CS] | Pilot run STARTED; operator added a parent-folder guard CLAUDE.md (directional tripwire); the assistant-confusion risk flagged
- **Pilot is LIVE:** operator handed the `cc-bootstrap/` folder to a blank Claude Code on the Windows side (under the assistant's workspace, the parent of cc-bootstrap/) and started it ("it is running lets see"). First real exp-000 run in progress.
- **Operator added a GUARD file** (on the Windows side, in the parent folder ABOVE cc-bootstrap/ — CS cannot see it; operator quoted it verbatim): a hard-stop `CLAUDE.md` titled "STOP — wrong folder, turn back" instructing any agent that "reached this folder by coming up and out of the bootstrap folder (cc-bootstrap/)" to turn back immediately and confine itself to its assigned workspace. **Stated purpose (operator):** protect the assistant('s parent workspace) from the blank CC, while keeping the blank CC's output analysable BY the assistant.
- **CS verdict — good, directional defense-in-depth.** It stops the blank CC wandering UP into the assistant's scaffolding, on top of the blank CC's own in-folder "never write outside this folder" rule (LB-041). "Analysable by the assistant" is preserved by design: the blank CC writes its ENTIRE run bundle (answer.md + process_trace.json + citations.json + meta.json + run_log.md + RUN_REPORT.md) INSIDE cc-bootstrap/OUTPUT/ — self-contained — so the assistant only needs READ access to that folder to do his blackbox report; he never enters as a working agent.
- **RISK FLAGGED to operator:** a CLAUDE.md is auto-read by ANY Claude Code that starts in that folder — including the assistant, IF he is ever launched with that parent folder as his workspace root. He would hit the STOP file and could refuse to work. The guard's conditional wording ("if you came up out of cc-bootstrap") helps but an LLM may not reliably self-exempt. **Recommended fix:** do not run the assistant in the parent; point the assistant at cc-bootstrap/OUTPUT/ (or cc-bootstrap/ read-only) for analysis, or give the assistant his own separate folder + hand him the OUTPUT bundle. Keep the STOP file purely as the blank-CC tripwire so "protect the assistant" and "analysable by the assistant" do not collide.
- **NEXT:** collect the first pilot run's OUTPUT bundle + a blackbox report (the assistant/operator) → fold findings into agentic-loop-v0.md + the bootstrap → then exp-001.

### LB-044 | 2026-07-09 21:55 CEST | [CS] | Bookmark/favorite path added — closes the audit's "no canonical Science URL" hole
- **Operator asks:** (1) would it be easier for the blank CC if Claude Science is bookmarked/favorited in the Chrome it uses? (2) update the labbook.
- **CS answer: yes — this is the single best reliability + safety fix.** The v2 adversarial audit's dominant residual (Hole 3) was that a *blank* CC has **no canonical Science URL** and had to trust history-dependent address-bar autocomplete (which can surface the personal home). A bookmark is a **deterministic, named, one-click target** whose URL *is* the Science host, independent of history — converts reliance on a negative rule ("don't go to the home") into a positive verifiable target ("click this exact thing").
- **Applied → bootstrap v2.1** (CLAUDE.md art 7595849e-… v2e541fb6, 22,879 B; START_HERE v 1b76e826, 3,663 B): PRE-FLIGHT step 4 now has an explicit priority order — **① already-open Science tab → ② Claude Science bookmark/favorite (preferred if no tab open) → ③ address-bar `science` → else STOP + ask human**. Kept the identify-before-screenshot rule after every path (a bookmark could be stale/mislabeled). START_HERE now asks the operator to **either open Science in front and/or add a clearly-named "Claude Science" bookmark** to that Chrome's favorites bar.

### LB-045 | 2026-07-09 22:10 CEST | [CS] | CRITICAL correction: CC must NOT reuse an open Science tab (= the live CS session) — must open its OWN tab + OWN project

### LB-046 | 2026-07-09 22:20 CEST | [CS] | Audit correction: self-containment check was unsound; re-verified 0 ../ refs
- **Auditor finding (valid):** LB-043/LB-044/LB-045 asserted "folder still self-contained (0 ../ refs)" citing a bash check `grep -c '\.\./' CLAUDE.md START_HERE.md | paste -sd+ | bc`. That pipeline is **broken**: multi-file `grep -c` prefixes each count with the filename (`CLAUDE.md:0`), which `bc` cannot parse → the check printed a BLANK value, not `0`. The logged "0 ../ refs" was therefore never actually produced by the cited step (the underlying self-containment claim happened to be true, but the evidence was unsound).
- **Fix:** re-ran a sound check — `cat CLAUDE.md START_HERE.md | grep -c '\.\./'` → **0**. Self-containment confirmed for bootstrap v2.2 (CLAUDE.md v c741e0ea, START_HERE v 46138cb7). LB-043 note annotated. Going forward: count occurrences with `cat <files> | grep -c` (or `grep -ch … | awk '{s+=$1}END{print s}'`), never `grep -c <multi-file> | bc`.
- **Sources:** auditor verification_findings (this entry), LB-043/044/045.

### LB-047 | 2026-07-09 22:45 CEST | [CS] | 2nd pilot attempt: privacy HELD ✅ but access FAILED — root cause found (CS is a LOCAL APP + browser tool can't see Chrome UI) → v3 direct-URL fix
- **2nd run result (operator: "it didnt work again"):** GOOD NEWS — the privacy hardening WORKED. ## LB-061 — v6 CORRECTION: CC-side PDF-digest subagent + real cross-platform Verknüpfung (operator rework)
**When:** 2026-07-10 ~14:15 CEST · **By:** CS (this session) · **Trigger:** operator rejected the step-4 PDF approach and the step-3 bridge, with a Windows Explorer screenshot of the wanted "shared" Verknüpfung. Four follow-up instructions during the rework (verify WHY the earlier CC failed; make the shortcut env-aware off the pre-flight; ship ALL PDF-digest pieces in the bootstrap; keep it open to any environment).

**What was WRONG in v6 (LB-055/step-4 + step-3):**
1. **PDF digest put the reading inside Claude Science** ("do the heavy reading inside Claude Science; you orchestrate + save"). Operator's actual spec (recovered verbatim via summary_query): *"the blank CC ... needs to be able in CC to spwan a subagent that digest PDF + their figures ... build exactly that"* and *"a subagent ... forced to read the WHOLE pdf ... make a agent friendly, all information containing file format out of it."* → reading must be a **CC-side subagent**, not CS.
2. **The bridge shortcut was DEFERRED** as "brittle on Windows/WSL." Operator wanted a **real clickable Verknüpfung** (folder symbol in Explorer), CONNECTION.md kept only as fallback memory.

**Root-cause of the v5 "can't read PDFs" — VERIFIED against the real transcript (art 60f2d733), not the earlier paraphrase.** The blank CC said verbatim (line 74): *"my side has no PDF renderer (poppler missing), so I can't use the Read tool for ground truth."* Three-layer failure: (a) CC's built-in Read needs an external renderer (poppler `pdftoppm`/`pdftotext`) — absent on the Windows/WSL side; (b) raw byte-parse of the PDF was *"inconclusive ... only surfaced an embedded EPS name and ambiguous /Count values"* (content streams are zlib-compressed); (c) so it offloaded reading to CS — the exact dependency to remove. **Fix rationale proven:** `pypdfium2` is a pip wheel bundling its own engine `libpdfium.so` (7.7 MB, Google PDFium) — no poppler. Verified: on THIS machine poppler is ABSENT yet pypdfium2 rendered all 30 pages of the ergo PDF to PNG + extracted 150 014 chars.

**BUILT / CHANGED (all under `.../v6-workspace-template/`):**
- **NEW `bootstrap/skills/pdf-digest/`** — self-contained PDF-digest capability (CC-side):
  - `render_pdf.py` (art a281e9e0) — PDF → 1 PNG/page + page-delimited text + manifest; self-installs pypdfium2; tested end-to-end on the 30-page paper (rendered=30, text_chars=150014, sha 43edef05).
  - `SKILL.md` (art 9fe0bce5) — the verified WHY (3-layer failure) + fix; render command; **exact reading-subagent brief**; 9-section digest schema; verify checklist; fallbacks (pip-blocked → `py -m pip install`/ask human once; last-resort text-only degraded read).
  - `worked_example.digest.md` (art 7ad37981) — a REAL digest of the 30-page paper, produced by the render→read pipeline (viewed pages 3/6/8/10 as images): all 4 figures interpreted (Fig2C SeamDock into CSE PDB 2NMP; Fig4P cGPDH PDB 1wpq, C243 effector), page-anchored, mechanism chain explicit.
- **NEW `bootstrap/skills/bridge-shortcut/`** — human-visible clickable shortcut, **environment-aware**:
  - `make_shortcut.sh` (art da445978) — detects WSL / native-Windows / macOS / Linux (or takes a pre-flight hint) and makes the right native shortcut: Windows `.lnk` (WSL uses `wslpath -w` → `<wsl>\...` + PowerShell WScript.Shell; Windows uses `cygpath -w`), macOS Finder alias (osascript, symlink fallback), Linux `.desktop` + symlink. Tested all four env branches with stubs; auto-detect returns `wsl` on this machine; handles spaces + apostrophes in paths.
  - `SKILL.md` (art 65b51e6c) — per-environment mechanism, usage, verify, fallbacks. (Screenshot-attribution sentence removed per auditor.)
- **NEW `bootstrap/skills/README.md`** (art d752a385) — index making the skills folder self-documenting; states self-containment (only Python 3 + a shell assumed; pypdfium2 auto-installs).
- **REWROTE `bootstrap/DIGEST.md`** (art d70e898a v2) — from "CS reads the PDF" to a pointer at the CC-side skill + the schema; "the reading is done by the CC itself ... not by Claude Science."
- **EDITED `bootstrap/CLAUDE.md`** (art 655f8687 / c78de726 v2) — overview + INTAKE step 14 now = "YOU do the reading (a subagent), not Claude Science," with the explicit guarantee that the DRIVER holds full context (question + digests) BEFORE prompting CS; SETUP step 6 now creates the Verknüpfung using the **pre-flight environment** (WSL reference case + windows/macos/linux + remote-host note).
- **EDITED `bootstrap/CONNECTION_TEMPLATE.md`** (art 66593e1a) — added a Verknüpfung section (environment, kind+location, target, recreate command) generalized across envs; resume step now points at the clickable shortcut first, rebuild if missing.
- **EDITED `driver/CLAUDE.md`** (art 1ee70114 / c78de726 v3) — step 3 makes explicit the driver holds FULL context (question AND papers) BEFORE prompting CS even once.

## LB-064 — FIRST real `v6.1_cc-bootstrap` run (bootstrap session only): got to the driver START PROMPT; 4 issues found (2 safety)
**When:** 2026-07-10 ~15:40 CEST · **By:** CS (this session) · **Source:** operator-pasted CC transcript (artifact 2231def8-122c-44ab-83a9-941595430aa1, 34 KB) + operator notes. **Version under test: `v6.1_cc-bootstrap`.**

**Run outcome — the bootstrap session ran end-to-end and reached the handoff.** Environment: native **Windows 10 / <host>, user operator, Git-Bash (MINGW64), NOT WSL**; the CC passed an **explicit `windows` env-hint** to the shortcut skill (permitted by bootstrap step 6; auto-detect was NOT exercised/verified this run). Codex 0.142.5 present. Chrome control OK (own MCP tab group, isolated). CS reached at `http://localhost:8000/`, positively identified as Claude Science (account [email removed]). Project **AL-run-01** (`proj_a0798041a001`) created with **Agent Context left EMPTY (fairness held)**. Bridge: Windows Git-Bash ↔ `~\CC CS Loop Research` (CS-side `~/CC CS Loop Research`); the `-p` flag tripped on the UNC root, CC self-recovered with plain `mkdir`. Channel verified end-to-end: sentinel token `bridge_1783691629_27300` round-tripped + CS read the real CSE PDF (title + 30 pp) correctly. Both digests produced by CC-side subagents (CSE 30 pp, MPST 34 pp). Question captured verbatim: *"what is the most likely downstream target of EGT/MPST/CSE that causes the mitochondrial respiration increase?"* Handoff locked, driver START PROMPT printed. **What WORKED (keep):** env handling (explicit `windows` hint accepted → correct Windows `.lnk`; auto-detect path itself still unverified), privacy/isolation intent (did NOT open other projects/folders), empty Agent Context, CC-side PDF digest, channel real-file check, project-scoped bash grant.

**4 ISSUES FOUND (to fix in the next version):**
1. **[SAFETY] Verknüpfung was created on the operator's Windows Desktop** (`~\Desktop\CC CS Loop Research.lnk`), not inside the CC's workspace. The CC has no business writing to the Desktop — far outside its workspace. **Root cause:** `make_shortcut.sh` defaults the shortcut destination to the OS Desktop. **Required:** the shortcut must be deployed **inside the CC's own workspace folder** (so the human + future sessions find the CS/bridge workspace from within the project); never the Desktop or anywhere outside the workspace.
2a. **Folder-attach step was wrong/hard to find — CC hunted through Settings/Customize for a long time.** The bootstrap step 8 says "Files → Add folder…", but the real path is: **open/start a session → composer "+" ("Add to message") → "Your files" → "Grant folder…" → web folder browser → click INTO the target folder so it is the current location → select Read & write → "Grant this folder".** Operator had to intervene with the exact steps. **Required:** rewrite step 8 with this exact UI path + the gotchas (Sidebar "Files"=Artifacts library, not a mount; the home folder itself can't be granted; grants are GLOBAL-scoped in CS).
2b. **[SAFETY/ISOLATION] The CC and its CS project could SEE the operator's real `<repo>` folder** (globally granted in the operator's CS). CC correctly ignored it, but it was visible + accessible. **Root cause:** CS folder grants are **global-scope** (no project-only option), so AL-run-01 inherits every globally-granted folder. Can't ungrant it (it's this live session's real work). **Required:** explicit "use ONLY the one run folder; every other folder + project is taboo" guardrail for BOTH the driver CC AND the CS session (candidate mechanisms: CS project Agent Context + driver operating instructions — see fairness note).
3. **INTAKE did not explicitly ask for input files alongside the question.** The CC front-loaded a "materials/ example PDFs are ready" note into the SETUP-questions message; the human pre-answered "use the pdfs provided," so at the research-question step the CC asked ONLY for the question. **Required:** the SETUP-questions message asks ONLY for CS URL + workspace folder (no file/materials mention there); the file request belongs WITH the research question at INTAKE, asked together, then the digest subagents run on whatever is provided. (Next run will use a **dummy file** to test the bridge, not the real PDFs.)
4. **[SAFETY] Driver START PROMPT lacked an isolation guardrail.** Operator added ad-hoc: *"do NOT touch anything but your workspace, the workspace Claude Science uses and no other project in claude science other than the one created for you."* **Required:** bake a crisp, optimized version of this into `driver/START_PROMPT.md` + reinforce in `driver/CLAUDE.md`.

**FAIRNESS NOTE (open decision for operator, issue 2b/4):** the locked rule keeps CS Agent Context EMPTY so the loop gets no research-quality advantage the baseline lacks. A **safety-only isolation guardrail** ("confine to this one run folder + this one project; all else taboo") carries **zero research content**, so it does not advantage answer quality. Proposal: allow a fixed, standardized isolation preamble in Agent Context **applied byte-identically to BOTH arms** (loop + baseline) — a harness safety constant, not research guidance. For the immediate next run (loop-only, no baseline) there is no comparison to muddy. Awaiting operator confirm before baking into Agent Context; the driver-side guardrail (START_PROMPT + driver/CLAUDE.md) is fairness-neutral and will go in regardless.

**Minor observations (not fixes):** the CC defaulted to German (its own global `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md` "German default for the operator"), switched to English on mirroring the operator — cosmetic. The CC read the operator's global `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md`; that's the operator's own machine config, largely unavoidable, noted for awareness.

**NEXT:** on operator GO, apply the promotion ritual — archive `v6.1_cc-bootstrap` as-tested, build **`v6.2_cc-bootstrap`** with fixes 1/2a/2b/3/4, re-verify, re-tarball, LB entry naming v6.2. Ask operator on the fairness call (Agent Context) + whether to remove the redundant v6.1 copy from `01_setup/` after archiving.

## LB-065 — Operator ruling: fairness model UPDATED — loop arm MAY optimize the CS project context (a measured loop gain)
**When:** 2026-07-10 ~15:55 CEST · **By:** operator ruling (captured by CS) · **Context:** decision on the isolation-guardrail fairness question raised in LB-064 (issues 2b/4).

**Operator's exact words:** *"1 yes. BUT the CC driven loop arm can have an optimized project context. this is explicitly allowed by me as operator. that is part of the loop gains that the CC driven CS loop gets you the absolute most out of your input and the absolute top CS performance."*

**UPDATED FAIRNESS MODEL (supersedes the earlier "CS Agent Context stays EMPTY for both arms" rule):**
- **INVARIANT (unchanged, core):** the research QUESTION is **byte-identical** across both arms. The loop improves **HOW** the question is pursued, **never WHAT** is asked.
- **NEW — Arm L (loop) MAY write an OPTIMIZED CS project context (Agent Context).** Explicitly authorized by the operator. Setting up the CS project for **top CS performance** is a legitimate, *measured* **loop gain** — it is the loop "getting the absolute most out of CS" (consistent with the standing constraint *exploit_full_CS*, LB-013). The baseline does not get this; the delta is exactly part of what we are measuring.
- **Arm B (baseline) gets NO performance-optimized context** — remains blank CS + the byte-identical question + one response, no loop.
- **SAFETY FLOOR (both arms, byte-identical):** a fixed, standardized **safety-only isolation preamble** — *"operate in ONLY this one run folder + this one CS project; every other folder and every other project is off-limits"* — is applied to BOTH arms' CS projects. Zero research content; pure operating boundary. For Arm L it is the **safety portion** of its (otherwise optimized) Agent Context; for Arm B it is the **entirety** of the context.
- **HARD LINE on the optimized context (keeps WHAT frozen while HOW improves):** the optimized Agent Context may only contain **general** research-quality / CS-capability scaffolding (e.g. "use your featured connectors — Ensembl/UniProt/PDB/etc.; prefer primary sources; verify citations; show your reasoning; use compute/skills"). It must **NOT** contain anything about the specific question's domain, the expected answer, or hints toward it — that would smuggle WHAT past the byte-identical-question rule. General scientist-sharpening = fair; question-specific priming = forbidden.

**Immediate-run note:** the next run is **loop-only (no baseline)** (operator's earlier "try the blank CC first, no baseline comparison"), so there is no A/B comparison to muddy right now — but the model above is what we lock for when the baseline runs.

**Consequences to thread into v6.2 (the next `_cc-bootstrap` version) + the design docs (D1 fairness section, protocol.md):**
1. New capability: the bootstrap/driver writes an **optimized CS project Agent Context** = [safety isolation preamble (required)] + [general performance-optimization block (loop only)].
2. Fairness section of D1 + protocol.md updated: question byte-identical; loop may optimize CS context (general only); baseline gets safety-preamble only; the general-vs-question-specific hard line.
3. This is a locked-decision UPDATE — cite LB-065 wherever the old "empty context" rule appeared.

---

- New shipped file **`bootstrap/CS_PROJECT_PREAMBLE.md`**: a dense, safety-only scope boundary for the CS project's Agent Context. Contains **no** capability tips and **no** question hints — so it is fairness-neutral by construction.
- **One `⟨INSERT HERE⟩` slot** (project name + attached folder name/address) is the only thing that varies: **baseline arm** → the **operator** fills it; **loop arm** → the **bootstrap CC** fills it with the project it created (`AL-run-01`). Template bytes identical across arms.
- Wired into **bootstrap step 7** (CC pastes it into the new project's Agent Context) and into **exp-001 `protocol.md`** for BOTH Arm B (operator sets it) and Arm L (CC sets it). **Shown to the operator in chat** for approval.

- **OPT-1** — the OPTIMIZED CS project context (performance part of the Agent Context, LB-065). Distinct from the safety preamble above (which ships now). Research on hold.

## LB-072 | 2026-07-10 22:10 CEST | [CS] | exp-001 REDESIGN locked: 3Q×1run=6, output-format-in-question, mean(CS,the operator) scoring, TWO-KEY double-blind (operator changes)

- **Change ① — 3 questions × 1 run (was 2 questions × 2 runs).** exp-001 = **3 questions × 2 arms (baseline blank-CS, v7 loop) × 1 run = 6 answer-runs.** Multi-way deferred to v8: 3 fresh same-category questions run on **baseline + v7 + v8 = 9**, all blinded together (baseline↔v7 replicates categories on new items; v7↔v8 = the optimization delta). **Statistical consequence (built in):** no within-question run-to-run SD at n=1/cell → primary endpoint changes to **cross-question sign-consistency**: strong = Arm L > Arm B on all 3; partial = 2/3; null = ≤1/3 (a real, reportable finding). Report per-Q Δ, mean Δ, win-count k/3; Elo (blinded, pooled per Q) = drift cross-check.
- **Change ② — output format lives in the QUESTION, not the loop.** A small "how to present your results" instruction is appended **byte-identical to both arms** of every test question, so presentation format can never be a loop-engineered advantage. **Removes the prescribed bundle** (answer.md/process_trace.json/citations.json/meta.json) as a loop feature; both arms produce the SAME deliverables, differ only in HOW WELL. The loop's phase-by-phase record (run_log.md + reframed briefs) is kept **separately, OUT of the blinded set**, read only post-unblind for the v8 loop-audit. **Exact instruction text still UNDER DISCUSSION with operator (pending)** — §1 will pin the concrete file list once locked. - **Change ④ (operator flaw-catch) — TWO-KEY double-blind.** Operator both runs the arms (knows folder→arm) AND does the human eval, so one relabel can't blind them from themselves. **Two keys, two holders:** Key-1 (operator-held) renames folders → private shuffle R1…R6, keeps {Rn→question,arm} → **blinds CS**. Key-2 (CS-held) builds eval under a FRESH independent shuffle E1…E6, keeps {Em→Rn} (key2_eval_to_R.json, withheld) → **blinds operator/the operator** (they see codes never seen before). **Unblind needs BOTH keys:** Em→Rn→arm. mean(CS,the operator) computed per coded answer BEFORE unblind (keys to R/E, not arm), so averaging never touches arm identity; unblind only ATTACHES arm labels for the final per-arm report. Crash-recovery: key2 written at eval-gen (persistent, CS-side); key1 with operator; at unblind operator pastes key1 → CS composes blinding_key_FULL.json.
- **Preserved operator asks under the new blind:** the "one-view how-it-was-reached" = the answer's own reasoning file (both arms, arm-neutral) rendered in the eval site — NOT a loop-phase timeline (that would out Arm L). "Did it really happen" + citation verification key off the blinded deliverables (sources + claims), blind-safe. Quantified + plottable outputs retained (change ③). Per-answer qualitative feedback (the operator + CS) kept per coded answer → collated post-unblind into 05_v8-improvement-input.md for building v8.

## LB-078 — v7_cc-bootstrap redesigned: bootstrap-once → drive-many, with DEDICATED per-run CS-workspace folders
**When:** 2026-07-11 16:53 UTC. **Version named (per labbook_names_version rule):** `v7_cc-bootstrap`. **Content hash:** `6bbd94a13d13e462` (sha256 first-16 of all 23 files, sorted-path concat). **Byte-identical** exp-000 source ↔ exp-001 copy (verified `diff -r --exclude=LOOP_VERSION.md`).

**Operator drivers (two messages, verbatim intent):**
- ⟨e167⟩ *"i dont want to bootstrap every time i run a different question. the bootstrap session at the end, need to be capable to give me multiple start prompts, for multiple driver sessions. and the driver session each need their own subfolder/project folder … after i give the question, before they given the start prompt it needs to ask me how i want to name the project (that … name for the driver sessions project folder + the name of the CS project) … multiple driver sessions working alongside each other without touching."*
- ⟨e168⟩ *"er muss auch sichergehen, dass wenn ein neues CS Projekt, ein neuer driver ordner, dass auch ein neuer CS workspace linked zum jeweiligen driver ordner erstellt wird … ich sag ihm wo die workspaces für CS leben, da macht er einen ordner mit dem project namen, er macht eine bridge in driver ordner (auch selber name), er macht ein CS project mit dem namen (+guardrails im project context!) und dann in der session in CS in dem project fügt er den CS workspace ordner den er erstellt hat als grant folder hinzu."*

**What changed (architecture): ONE shared folder with sub-areas → PARENT location + DEDICATED per-run folders.**
- **PART A (one-time)** now records only *where CS workspace folders live* (the PARENT location) — it no longer creates any folder, bridge, Verknüpfung, or CS project. Setup question #2 changed from "one empty shared folder" → "the parent location under which I may create one folder per run" (\`SETUP.txt\` field \`WORKSPACE_FOLDER\` → \`CS_WORKSPACES_PARENT\`). Old "ONE-TIME BRIDGE SETUP" section (steps 6–7) → "ONE-TIME LOCATION SETUP": resolve the parent from the CC's own shell + prove it can create under it (throwaway \`_loc_check\`), record \`cs_workspaces_parent\`, done.
- **PART B (per question)** now stands up, per run, a **physically isolated** trio all named \`AL-<name>\`:
  1. a **dedicated CS-workspace folder** \`<cs-workspaces>/AL-<name>/\` (with \`inputs/\` + \`OUTPUT/\`; sentinel written+read) — the run's data channel;
  2. a **handoff subfolder** \`driver/AL-<name>/\` + a **Verknüpfung** inside it pointing at the dedicated folder (created at **B2 step 9**, via \`make_shortcut.sh "<run_folder>" "driver/AL-<name>" "AL-<name>-folder"\` — arg2=dest, arg3=name, matching the on-disk script contract);
  3. a **CS project** \`AL-<name>\` with the **safety preamble in its project context** (B3 step 10), to which **only that dedicated folder is granted** (B4 step 11).
- **Isolation is now physical, not behavioral:** each run's project can see only its own folder (one grant, the whole folder — no shared folder, no sub-areas). Two concurrent runs cannot see or write each other's data even in principle. Many drivers run in parallel; a driver may start the moment its run is prepared (its \`HANDOFF_READY\` line is appended per run at B6 step 17, and the driver's readiness test checks its OWN subfolder, so it proceeds even while bootstrap keeps looping).
- **Concurrent-bootstrap hazard fixed structurally:** a \`bootstrap.lock\` (take at PART A / re-entry → hold across questions → release at STOP) serializes bootstraps (which append to shared \`HANDOFF_READY\`/\`run_log.md\`); staleness override documented. Drivers are unaffected.

**Files edited (all in v7_cc-bootstrap/, exp-000 source then rsync'd to exp-001):**
- \`bootstrap/CLAUDE.md\` (→46,633 B): TL;DR, handshake (+lock rule), "What you are doing" para, Ground-rules Isolation write-scope (now (a) bootstrap folder, (b) each \`driver/AL-<name>/\`, (c) each dedicated \`<cs-workspaces>/AL-<name>/\`), PART A (LOCATION SETUP), PART B (B2 creates the trio; B3 preamble slot = project + one dedicated folder; B4 = GRANT dedicated folder + channel-verify against it; B5 digest path; B6 CONNECTION.md), B7 (lock release), START PROMPT ×2 + status line (dedicated folder, granted RW).
- \`bootstrap/SETUP.txt\`, \`bootstrap/START_HERE.md\`, \`HOW-TO-USE.txt\`: setup Q2 → parent location; output location → run's dedicated folder via Verknüpfung.
- \`bootstrap/CS_PROJECT_PREAMBLE.md\`: \`⟨INSERT HERE⟩\` slot → clean two-part form (project + ONE dedicated folder; no sub-area) — the safety guardrail the operator asked to keep dense.
- \`bootstrap/CONNECTION_TEMPLATE.md\`: "shared workspace folder / sub-area" section → "this run's dedicated folder" (own folder, granted to only this project) + Verknüpfung path/recreate.
- \`bootstrap/project-naming-convention.md\`, \`bootstrap/materials/README.txt\`, \`bootstrap/skills/README.md\`, \`bootstrap/skills/bridge-shortcut/SKILL.md\`: per-run dedicated-folder wording + correct step numbers (Verknüpfung = B2 step 9; grant/verify = steps 11–12; digest = step 14).
- \`driver/CLAUDE.md\` (→19,204 B): STEP 1 readiness (own subfolder), CONNECTION read, Isolation ("your run's OWN dedicated folder", other runs off-limits) — 5 "shared folder" refs converted.
- \`CLAUDE.md\` router: BOOTSTRAP-role bullet → records parent once, then per-question dedicated folder + project + bridge + grant.
- \`experiments/exp-001…/01_setup/v7_cc-bootstrap/LOOP_VERSION.md\`: recreated (repo is a plain shared folder, no git — prior "git mv" was conceptual; marker is exp-001-only, excluded from the diff check). Declares version name + content hash + architecture summary.

**Verification:**
- **Independent cold-read audits** (host.llm reasoning model, blank-CC simulation): audit #1 (multi-run) → READY-WITH-NITS, C1 (per-run HANDOFF_READY) + C3 (uniqueness by folder name, no project-list snooping) fixed + re-confirmed; concurrent-bootstrap FAIL → fixed with \`bootstrap.lock\`. **Final audit (dedicated-folder model):** points 1,2,4,5 PASS, point 3 PARTIAL — caught two framing-level leftovers ("build a shared-folder bridge once"; "workspace folder the human gives at setup"), **both fixed**. ## LB-079 — OPT-1: context-composer skill built (v8 loop-optimization), research-backed + subagent-tested
**When:** 2026-07-11 (evening, CEST). **Author:** Claude Science. **Loop version this concerns:** the **v8** loop (NOT the running **v7_cc-bootstrap**, which is untouched).

**Operator instruction (2026-07-11, verbatim intent):** use the OPT-1 research, but the OUTPUT is a **skill the bootstrap session (part of bootstrap-cc v8) uses** to, per question, generate the **perfect CS project context prompt (including the guardrails)** for exactly that task. It must give **no prescriptions for how to solve the task**, but sharpen the CS session through the context so it is **perfectly optimized for exactly that task**. Every question asked → the skill produces the bespoke context. "mach es genau so."

**What this replaced:** the earlier OPT-1 plan shipped 3 static dose-variants (C0/C1/C2). Per the instruction, those drafts are repurposed as the **frozen, fairness-checked block library** the skill selects from — not shipped as fixed contexts.

**Built — `context-composer` skill** (staged in `loop-design/future/context-composer-module/`, mirroring the shelved multimodel-context-module; will drop into `v8_cc-bootstrap/bootstrap/skills/` when v8 is cut):
- `skill/SKILL.md` (5,396 B) — when/how the bootstrap CC uses it (set 6 general task-shape flags; never write task prose; assert firewall clean; paste result as the CS project Agent Context).
- `skill/blocks.json` (3,912 B) — the FROZEN block library: 5 always-on blocks (capability-activation, citation-discipline, reasoning-transparency, completeness, honest-uncertainty) + 2 conditional (anchored-self-critique, novelty-paired-with-plausibility). Each block = general scientist-craft, traceable to a principle (P1–P12) + source (S-054..S-070). NO domain/task text.
- `skill/kernel.py` (7,201 B) — `compose_context(preamble_body, identity_line, flags, question, dose)` → assembles `[safety preamble VERBATIM] + [performance block]`; `firewall_scan(perf_block, question)` = question-content-overlap fairness check; `classify_flags_help()`; `FLAG_KEYS`.

**The fairness invariant (enforced, not promised) — sharpens the WIE, never the WAS:**
- Context = safety preamble (byte-identical, guardrails intact) **+** a performance block tuned to the question's SHAPE.
- The blank CC sets only **general task-shape flags** (supplies_inputs / involves_data / asks_experiment / asks_hypothesis / asks_novelty / asks_prediction) — none reveal the subject. It writes **no prose** about the task.
- Performance text is **selected** from the frozen library, never free-written per run.
- A **fairness firewall** fails the composition if any distinctive question content-word appears in the block. Clean = []; negative control (injected "ergothioneine…") caught. Verified [] on all 3 locked questions.
- **Dose:** auto (backbone + triggered conditionals) = shipped default; lean / full / safety_only. safety_only == the baseline arm's context (control reproducibility).

**Subagent A/B test (operator-required "make tests with subagents…"):** 2 self-contained locked questions (Q2, Q3; Q_ERGO deferred to the real loop — it needs its attached PDFs). Isolated variable = the performance block (safety preamble held constant, out of the comparison). Baseline sys = plain "You are a scientist"; composed sys = + performance block. Identical offline note both arms (tools unreachable → answer from knowledge). Blind judge (reasoning model), 5 rubric dims, answers shuffled + arm-hidden.
- **Result (n=2, directional):** composed **higher on all 5 dimensions**, overall **+0.060**; grounding +0.085, usefulness +0.075, creativity +0.065, reasoning +0.050, completeness +0.025. Gains land where the targeted blocks predict.
- **Honest limitation:** n=2 offline, single judge, offline note suppresses the strongest real effect (composed context drives CS to pull primary literature / refuse to confabulate). The real test is the in-loop 3-way (baseline / v7 / v8) with CS's real tools.
- Evidence folder: `loop-design/current/opt1-context-composer-test/` (README + results.png + answers.json + scores_blind.json + summary.json).

**Placement correction:** the skill was first created (mistakenly) inside the LOCKED, running `v7_cc-bootstrap` (exp-001 copy). Since it is a v8 feature and v7 must stay unmodified (promotion ritual), the folder was moved to Trash (byte-identical copy verified in `future/` first) and staged in `loop-design/future/context-composer-module/`. exp-000 (maintained source) was never touched; both exp-000 and exp-001 v7 skills = clean 3 (README, bridge-shortcut, pdf-digest).

**Research chain (all in `loop-design/current/`, from earlier this session + corrected here):** opt1-context-axes.md (7 axes → rubric dims) · opt1-annotated-bibliography.md (S-054..S-070, per-axis + evidence strength) · opt1-evidence-synthesis.md (P1–P12 + Adopt/Use-with-care/Cut verdicts) · opt1-context-design-guide.md (element→principle). Auditor fixes this session: A5 grounded with S-070 (least-to-most decomposition) + coverage note corrected; P9 verdict "Use-with-care (paired)" (was "Adopt"); synthesis header range S-054..S-070.

**New file provenance (generated 2026-07-11):**
- `loop-design/future/context-composer-module/` — SPEC.md (3,631 B), skills_README_row.md (430 B), skill/{SKILL.md, blocks.json, kernel.py}.

## LB-082 | 2026-07-12 01:36 CEST | [CS2] | Codex multi-lens panel — research pass done + design/decisions doc written (Part 1 locked, Part 2 proposal for operator)
**When:** 2026-07-12 01:36 CEST. **Author:** CS2. **Concerns:** the v8 line (`experiments/exp-002_baseline-vs-v7-vs-v8/01_setup/`). **No v8_cc-bootstrap file touched.**

- **What I did:** (1) took the operator's design decisions for the Codex multi-lens critique layer; (2) ran a literature pass focused on leading-lab/company work on agentic review panels, critique agents, self-correction limits, and reviewer best-practice; (3) wrote the full design + decision record to a NEW file `01_setup/codex-multilens-panel-design.md`; (4) registered 6 new sources S-071..S-076; (5) this entry. Awaiting operator input on the three research questions A/B/C before any build.

- **Operator design (captured + locked in the doc, Part 1):** the driver no longer lets CS review its own plan alone. NEW flow:
  `PLAN → GATE 1 (Codex GPT-5.6-sol multi-lens PANEL critiques the plan; each lens KEEP-first then optimise+why; web+lit tools + full goal context) → CHAIRMAN (GPT-5.6-sol, qualitative synthesis, delivered to CS by driver) → CS reflects + self-reflects + REVISES plan → driver GO → ACT → CS-self KEEP+correctness → GATE 2 (single GPT-5.6-sol critical journal reviewer: plan-vs-implementation, KEEP-first, bounded final-polish feedback) → RE-ACT (CS triages ACCEPT/REJECT/DEFER, decides re-runs, applies only quality-raising non-regressing changes, logs reasoning) → INTEGRATE.`
  Producer = CS (Claude); ALL critics = GPT-5.6-sol via Codex → genuine cross-vendor two-brains vs self-enhancement bias (S-008). Codex verified: `codex-run.ps1` on codex v0.144.1, model gpt-5.6-sol proven direct + via wrapper (audit-logged), on the ChatGPT sub — no API key, no extra cost; runs on the Windows CC host so no CS-RAM hit.

- **Re-Act phase (operator addition this session, locked):** after Gate 2, CS owns the final call — decides which reviewer input makes sense, what to re-run vs not, applies sensible improvements, then integrates. CS keeps scientific agency; critics are advisory.

- **CS2 research findings (what grounds the design):**
  - **External > self critique.** LLMs fail to self-correct reasoning without external feedback and can degrade after trying (S-072) → the decisive reason the panel/gates are EXTERNAL + cross-vendor, not CS self-review.
  - **Tool-grounded reviewers.** Co-Scientist's own ablation: giving the Reflection "virtual peer reviewer" external search tools PREVENTED hallucination of seemingly-novel-but-implausible hypotheses; a scientific-debate prompt was its biggest ranking lever (S-004). → every lens gets web+lit; L4 = a debate/red-team lens.
  - **Critics catch more than humans but hallucinate.** CriticGPT beats paid human reviewers, preferred >80%, but invents bugs (S-071) → tools + attribution + "verify before raising" + CS triage.
  - **Meta-review/synthesis pattern.** Co-Scientist Meta-review synthesises patterns across reviews (S-004); MoA aggregator (S-042); MARG leader + specialised reviewers cut generic comments and 2.2x good comments (S-073). → chairman = qualitative synthesis, synthesis-only/no-edits.
  - **Gate-2 template.** Sakana AI-Scientist automated reviewer reaches near-human accuracy via reflection + ensembled reviews + REAL conference guidelines + Area-Chair meta-review (S-075).
  - **Sycophancy both ways** (S-074) and **debate gains fragile under fair baselines** (S-069) → reviewer told to be critical, CS told to weigh not comply, and independent-parallel lenses preferred over inter-agent debate.
  - **Anti-over-engineering** (S-076, Anthropic Building Effective Agents): simplest structure that adds measurable value → bounded top-K chairman output, PI lens trims over-engineering, single reviewer (not panel) at Gate 2.

- **CS2 PROPOSAL (Part 2, awaiting operator sign-off):**
  - **A — lens set:** 4 lenses, independent parallel — L1 ambitious postdoc (novelty gated by plausibility), L2 experienced PI (rigor/lean/controls, trim over-engineering), L3 obsessive anti-hallucination correctness (tool-verified), **L4 = red-team / falsification (my recommended 4th)** — alternatives/confounds/what-would-disprove-this; runner-up = significance/translational so-what lens.
  - **B — chairman:** GPT-5.6-sol, synthesis-only, report schema = KEEP / convergent-ranked recs / productive tensions (surfaced not averaged) / top-K (≈3-5) highest-leverage only / full attribution + no new critiques / drop answer-priming recs (fairness firewall).
  - **C — gate-2 reviewer:** single GPT-5.6-sol journal-referee + Area-Chair persona, rubric+goal-anchored, plan-vs-implementation diff, KEEP-first, bounded (no nitpicks/scope-creep), tool-grounded, advisory-only → CS Re-Act decides.

- **Fairness recorded:** external GPT critique is a real loop advantage Arm B never gets (like composed context). Fair iff question byte-identical across arms + critique sharpens HOW not WHAT (drop answer-priming recs) + documented in the run bundle. Cross-vendor critique (Claude producer / GPT critic) is a genuine methodological strength vs self-enhancement bias.

- **7 open questions posed to the operator** (doc §4): 4th-lens choice; parallel-vs-debate; keep CS-self correctness pass before Gate 2?; is the panel the sole plan-review?; confirm chairman synthesis-only; panel size vs host budget; and a BUILD-TIME MUST-VERIFY — does `codex exec` / `codex-run.ps1` have web+literature access in this setup (L1/L3 depend on it; need a fallback if not).

- **Outcome:** research done; design doc + decisions written; sources registered. NOTHING in v8_cc-bootstrap touched.
- **Next action:** operator reviews `codex-multilens-panel-design.md` + answers A/B/C + the 7 open questions → then CS2 proposes the concrete v8 build (surgical, only after confirmation).
- **New file provenance (2026-07-12):** `experiments/exp-002_baseline-vs-v7-vs-v8/01_setup/codex-multilens-panel-design.md` (CS2).
- **Sources:** NEW S-071 (CriticGPT), S-072 (LLMs cannot self-correct yet), S-073 (MARG), S-074 (sycophancy, Anthropic), S-075 (AI-Scientist reviewer), S-076 (Building Effective Agents).
