## LB-082b | 2026-07-12 01:35 CEST | [CS] | exp-001 BLIND SCORING complete — all 6 answers scored real-mode, eval site built (Key-2), blind analysis + figures shipped

**When:** 2026-07-12 ~01:35 CEST. **Author:** Claude Science — session 1 (CS1). **Experiment:** exp-001_baseline-vs-v0-loop (arms B raw blank-CS / L blank-CC+v0-loop, 3 questions × 2 arms × 1 run = 6 answer-runs). **Loop of record:** v7_cc-bootstrap. **Numbering note:** this is LB-082 — LB-081 was claimed by the parallel CS2 workstream (Codex panel / v8); my exp-001 work follows it in sequence, no content overlap.

**Context / baton:** operator delivered the 6 real exp-001 presentation folders (R1–R6) into `experiments/exp-001…/02_results/`, holding **Key-1** (R-code → arm). Plan approved: *"make sure this is done professionally and documented extensively in submission quality — this part (how we score results) will be a core part of the submission."* This entry is that documentation.

### What was done (6 steps)

**1. Blind manifest.** Classified the 6 answers by QUESTION only (blind-safe): Q_ERGO = {R2,R3}, Q2 = {R4,R6}, Q3 = {R1,R5}. The blind mechanism = **`arm = code`** — each answer scored independently under its R-code; no L−B delta is computable until Key-1 is applied. Scored bundle = `result.md` + `reasoning.md`. Extraction scan: 29 unique PMIDs, 33 DOIs, 16 dataset accessions across the six. Files: `02_results/scoring/manifest_blind.json`, `extraction_scan.json`.

**2. Connector pre-fetch (real grounding).** Via `host.mcp` PubMed + a `host.llm`/CrossRef pass: **29/29 cited PMIDs resolved**, **all 33 DOIs confirmed real** (19 via PubMed incl. the two Cell Metabolism ergothioneine papers S-015/S-016, + 14 via CrossRef covering the origin-of-life physics/chemistry literature and preprints), **all 16 dataset accessions resolve** to the correct entities (PDB 7SUS/8S9P, UniProt P35414/O15146/ergo-pathway + Wood–Ljungdahl enzymes, GEO GSE167186/151066/163356/157585). **Zero fabricated citations or datasets across all six.** Novelty scored against broadened real queries (tight 0-hit queries would inflate novelty to 1.0). Unified snapshot: `02_results/scoring/connector_cache.json` (CHECKPOINT). **Infra learning:** the `repl` kernel has no direct network egress (proxy 403 even for NCBI/CrossRef) — `host.mcp` works via the host; direct HTTP must run in the python kernel. Logged for future scoring runs.

**3. Real-mode blind scoring.** Built `CachedAdapters(RealAdapters)` — cache-backed connector methods + real dataset-resolver/trace-recheck, inheriting live `host.llm` entailment/judge/compare. 3-persona reviewer panel (Rigor/Significance/Novelty), creativity panel, Elo — all live `host.llm`. **Integrity-cap bug found + fixed (major):** a first run capped ALL 6 grounding at 1 via a false-positive cascade (loose accession regex matching years/figure-numbers; trace-only PMIDs never pre-fetched; tokenless connector steps mislabeled "unverified"). Fix: (a) fetched all 19 trace-only PMIDs + 4 R5 trace-only DOIs — **every one REAL, zero fabrications**; (b) patched `verify_trace` to a 3-way logic **verified / unverified / asserted**, where a described connector step WITHOUT a re-checkable citation token is *asserted* (taken at face value, NOT a fabrication), and only a named PMID/DOI that fails to resolve is *unverified*. Result: **zero fabricated actions anywhere**; integrity settles honestly at cap 2 (low independently-verifiable fraction — uniform across answers, so unbiased).

**Blind scores (by code, no arm):**

Elo agrees with composite for Q2/Q3, **disagrees for Q_ERGO** (composite R2>R3 by 0.043; Elo flips it) — a genuine "too close to call from CS alone" signal, reported.

**4. the operator human-eval site (Key-2 — the second blind).** `make_eval_site.py` (operator-approved warm/light design) → `04_evaluation/eval_site.html`: 3 questions, 6 answer cards shuffled to A/B **per question** (seed 42); the operator scores 4 science dims + creativity-honesty + red flags + qualitative per answer + head-to-head per question; **process_trace excluded** (blind-safety); copy-to-clipboard capture. Self-contained (all 17 in-markdown figures inlined as base64, 0 external refs). **Blind-safety verified:** 0 R-codes in visible text (24 raw regex hits were base64 noise), only A/B shown, all "baseline" hits are scientific content ("baseline VWR", "GTEx baseline"). **Key-2** (`04_evaluation/key2_eval_to_R.json`, display-label → R-code) is CS-held and withheld from the operator until the operator's eval is in. Map: Q_ERGO A=R3/B=R2, Q2 A=R6/B=R4, Q3 A=R1/B=R5.

**5. Blind analysis + figures.** `02_results/scoring/BLIND_ANALYSIS.md` (arm-free, submission-grade) + 4 figures (`figs/fig_blind_*.png`): paired composites, per-dimension breakdown, **creativity-gate decomposition** (novelty × plausibility × reasoning-trace — the anti-hallucination gate made visible; R4 lowest at 0.12, gated on both weak plausibility 0.50 and weak reasoning-trace 0.50), and citation quality (R4 has most citations (33) but its verified-support 0.212 is essentially tied with R2's 0.20 at the bottom; R5 verifies best at 0.667 — **quality ≠ quantity**). Blind CSVs: `scorecard_blind.csv` + `scorecard_long_blind.csv` (long format, one row per code × dim × scorer, arm=code, ready for the operator-merge).

**6. Operator's unblind stage (built + documented).** `01_setup/for-the operator/unblind_and_analyze.py` composes **Key-1 ∘ Key-2 → blinding_key_FULL.json**, backfills arm into the long scorecard, optionally merges the operator scores, then runs `make_analysis.py` → L−B endpoint (mean-Δ across questions + k/3) + per-dim/per-arm/per-category figures. Patched `make_analysis.py` (v3) so the endpoint is **scorer-adaptive**: CS-only interim delta immediately after Key-1, upgraded to combined(CS+the operator) once the operator merges (records `scorer` + `is_interim_cs_only`). Smoke-tested end-to-end with a synthetic random Key-1 (then deleted — no real unblinding persisted, blind intact). `04_evaluation/key1_R_to_arm.TEMPLATE.json` = the template the operator fills.

### The two-key double-blind (the method we demonstrate for submission)
- **Key-1 (operator-held):** R-code → arm (B/L). CS never sees it while scoring.
- **Key-2 (CS-held):** eval-label (A/B per question) → R-code. Operator/the operator never see it while evaluating.
- **Neither key alone reveals arm.** CS's 6 blind scores are frozen BEFORE any key is applied (no arm knowledge could influence them); the operator evaluates A/B blind. Final unblind = Key-1 ∘ Key-2 → arm, only then is the L−B endpoint computed. This is the blinding system the operator locked (LB-072/073) and asked to be a demonstrated submission method.

### Files generated (2026-07-12, all under `experiments/exp-001_baseline-vs-v0-loop/`)
- `02_results/scoring/`: manifest_blind.json, extraction_scan.json, connector_cache.json (checkpoint), BLIND_ANALYSIS.md, blind_scores/{R1..R6}.json + blind_results_full.json + elo_blind.json + scorecard_blind.csv + scorecard_long_blind.csv, figs/fig_blind_{composites,dimensions,creativity_gate,citation_quality}.png
- `04_evaluation/`: eval_site.html (Key-2 blinded, self-contained), key2_eval_to_R.json (CS-held), key1_R_to_arm.TEMPLATE.json (operator fills)
- `01_setup/for-the operator/unblind_and_analyze.py`; `01_setup/harness/make_analysis.py` (v3, scorer-adaptive endpoint)

- **Outcome:** exp-001 CS-side scoring COMPLETE and blind-safe; all artifacts saved. CS holds Key-2, is blind to arm.

The L−B verdict is the OPERATOR's stage — CS does not compute it while blind.

## LB-083 | 2026-07-12 02:10 CEST | [CS] | exp-001 Grounding & integrity cap CORRECTION — flat-2 bug fixed (operator-flagged)

**Trigger:** operator, doing the the operator eval, flagged that all six answers scored a flat **2** on "Grounding & integrity" and asked whether the scorer had a bug. It did — two cap bugs that collapsed the grounding scale. Investigated with data (per-answer decomposition of min(judge, citation_cap, integrity_cap)), root-caused both, fixed within the LOCKED rubric-v2 anchors, re-scored, regenerated all downstream artifacts. NOTE: "Reasoning & soundness" was NOT flat (varied 3.0–5.0); only Grounding was pinned.

**Root cause 1 — integrity cap used the wrong denominator (dominant; hit all 6).** `integrity_cap()` computed verified_fraction = verified_steps / **ALL** trace steps, where a step counts "verified" only if it embeds a resolvable PMID/DOI. Reasoning/analysis steps carry no citation token by nature, yet sat in the denominator → every trace scored 0.0–0.18, always below the 0.3 threshold → cap 2 for everyone regardless of soundness. This measured citation-density, not "did it really happen."
  **Fix:** denominator is now the CHECKABLE steps only (n_verified + n_unverified). A step naming no checkable artifact is "asserted" (taken at face value, per the LB-082b 3-way verify_trace logic), NOT a failure. Only a named artifact that fails to resolve is a hit. With zero fabricated actions anywhere, the trace now contributes no false cap.

**Root cause 2 — citation cap conflated "unverifiable" with "fabricated" (hit R2, R4).** `grounding_cap()` used entailment-support alone (supported/total). A citation that resolves to a real paper but whose abstract could not be fetched (all DOI-only refs) was scored "unsupported" — identical to a fabricated reference. But existence is ~100% (R2 5/5, R4 30/33, R5 9/9, R6 18/18; zero fabrications).
  **Fix:** cap is now EXISTENCE-AWARE. exist_rate<0.5 → cap 1 (fabrication signal, preserved); exist_rate<0.8 → cap 2; real sources (exist_rate≥0.8) → support lifts within the real band (≥0.9→5, ≥0.6→4, ≥0.3→3), with a floor of 3 when sources are real but support is unconfirmable ("partially grounded, some gaps" = rubric anchor 3). Fabricated/nonexistent references still crash to 1.

**Alignment to LOCKED anchors (rubric.json dimensions[0], operator-locked LB-075):** 2 = "few citations, some don't support / can't be verified"; 3 = "main claims cited to real sources and mostly verifiable, some gaps"; 4 = "real, on-point sources; datasets resolve and were used". The flat-2 was WRONG by the rubric's own text — R5 (9 real cites, 67% support, datasets resolve) is anchor 4, not 2.

**Result — grounding now discriminates (was flat 2):**
| Code | Q | grounding OLD→NEW | composite OLD→NEW | why |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| R1 | Q3 | 2→2 | 3.510→3.510 | 0 citations = unsupported (anchor 2) |
| R2 | Q_ERGO | 2→3 | 3.793→3.993 | 5 real cites, 20% support (anchor 3) |
| R3 | Q_ERGO | 2→2 | 3.750→3.750 | 0 citations |
| R4 | Q2 | 2→2 | 2.947→2.947 | panel judged grounding 2 (not a cap artifact) |
| R5 | Q3 | 2→4 | 3.591→3.991 | 9 real cites, 67% support, datasets resolve (anchor 4) |
| R6 | Q2 | 2→3 | 3.413→3.613 | 18 real cites, 56% support (anchor 3) |

**Composite vs Elo (post-fix, corrected):** composite and Elo AGREE on Q2 (R6) and Q3 (R5). They still DISAGREE on Q_ERGO — composite favours R2 (3.99 vs 3.75) while Elo ranks R3 first. The grounding-cap fix did NOT flip this; it is a genuine near-tie where the two aggregation methods weight the answers differently (Elo = direct pairwise text comparison; composite = weighted five-dimension sum). Both reported so the divergence is visible. (Correction: an earlier draft of this entry mis-stated that the fix made Q_ERGO agree — it does not; the report's own §3.4 table is authoritative.)

**Anti-hallucination preserved:** the harness dry-run suite still passes 13/13, INCLUDING "fabricated cites → grounding cap 1" and "trap grounding = 1". No arm labels were involved in the fix — uniform code applied to all six blind. The blind two-key discipline is intact; my scores are still frozen before Key-1.

**Files (all 2026-07-12, versioned):** harness `scoring/composite.py` (integrity_cap denominator fix, artifact 90ab17c0 v6) + `scoring/citations.py` (existence-aware grounding_cap, artifact d10afbf6 v2); re-scored `02_results/scoring/blind_scores/R{1..6}.json` (v2) + `scorecard_blind.csv` + `scorecard_long_blind.csv` + `blind_results_full.json` (v2); regenerated `figs/fig_blind_composites.png` + `fig_blind_dimensions.png` (v2); rewrote `BLIND_ANALYSIS.md` (v2, new §6 documenting this correction). elo_blind.json unchanged (Elo is text-pairwise, grounding-independent).

**Numbering note:** this is LB-083 (uniquely mine — CS2 skipped 083). My prior exp-001-scoring entry originally also landed on LB-082, colliding with [CS2]'s LB-082 Codex research-pass (both ~01:35). RESOLVED (LB-088): my blind-scoring entry was renamed **LB-082b** (append-only "b" suffix convention, as with LB-073b); CS2 keeps LB-082. References to my blind-scoring entry now read LB-082b. ## LB-087 | 2026-07-12 10:15 CEST | [CS] | exp-001 UNBLINDED — FINAL RESULT: v7 loop beats baseline (mean-Δ=+0.48, k=2/3)

**Trigger:** operator submitted the operator's completed evaluation (all 3 questions, A/B per question, science dims + honesty + qualitative) AND Key-1 (operator-held R-code→arm). Both keys now in hand → final two-key unblinding executed.

**Key-1 (operator, verbatim):** blank CS (B) = R3(ERGO), R1(Exerkine/Q3), R6(OriginOfLife/Q2); v7 loop (L) = R2(ERGO), R5(Q3), R4(Q2). Per question the eval-site "A" was always the B arm and "B" the L arm (coincidental to the seed-42 shuffle, verified via the composition, not assumed).

**Method executed:** `01_setup/for-the operator/unblind_and_analyze.py` — composed both keys, backfilled arm into the blind scorecard_long (was arm=code), merged the operator's science scores (keyed by R-code to avoid the bare-A/B label collision in the runner's optional remap), ran make_analysis.py → endpoint + 9 figures. Scores were FROZEN while blind (LB-082b/083); unblinding only attached arm labels — no score changed.

**ENDPOINT (combined mean(CS,the operator) composite — the locked headline):**
- **mean-Δ (L−B) = +0.476** across the 3 questions; **k = 2/3 wins**; verdict = positive (won most; inspect the loss).
- Per-question Δ: **Q3 (sarcopenia) +1.24** (biggest win), **Q_ERGO +0.42**, **Q2 (origin-of-life) −0.23** (the one loss).
- Honest power caveat retained: n=3×1, DESCRIPTIVE not powered; no p-value claimed. Contribution = the METHOD demonstrated end-to-end + a directional effect.

**Most important finding — the effect lives in the human-expert layer:**
- CS-harness-only endpoint: Δ = **+0.019** (arms indistinguishable to the automated panel — it scores both high and flat).
- Combined (CS+the operator): Δ = **+0.476** (loop wins clearly).
- the operator separates the arms in the loop's favour on every science dim (creativity B→L 2.0→3.67; usefulness 2.0→3.0; reasoning 3.0→3.67; completeness 3.0→3.67). **the operator's own head-to-head picked the LOOP on ALL 3 questions** (Q_ERGO medium, Q3 high, Q2 low) — unanimous expert preference; combined reads k=2/3 only because the CS panel flipped Q2. CS-vs-the operator agreement weak (Pearson r=+0.15, n=24 science-dim pairs); the operator ~0.9 pts harsher overall. → concrete v8 optimisation target: harsher/more-discriminating CS panel anchors (the current leniency compresses the very signal being measured).

**Per-question expert read (the operator, verbatim highlights):**
- **Q3 (L wins, high confidence):** loop answer (R5) — *"very strong answer, never heard of the NMJ improvement as an exercise mimetic strategy … i am impressed"*; baseline (R1) got a HALLUCINATION/overclaim flag — *"apelin is a known exerkine, drugs already exist … just lit scrape."* The clearest win.
- **Q_ERGO (L wins, medium):** loop (R2) — *"the differences in affinity and expression levels of downstream sulfur enzymes were real noveltys … CoQ ox/red readout … makes a lot of sense."* BOTH arms failed the pilot-experiment ask (overengineered mouse study, "not a pilot"). → loop improvement: design a small cheap model-system pilot first (e.g. Seahorse in cell culture).
- **Q2 (the operator picked the LOOP, low confidence; combined = the one B win):** the operator's own head-to-head chose the loop (R4) — *"seems to be deeper thought out … mapping out of all hypothesis was good"* — but flagged it *"very complicated to read and very long."* The COMBINED composite is the one that lands on B (−0.23), only because the CS panel scored B higher on Q2 (CS B 3.61 vs L 2.95) enough to outweigh the operator's low-confidence L pick (the operator L 2.4 vs B 2.0). So the operator swept all 3 (see below); k=2/3 is a CS-panel artifact on Q2, not a the operator loss. → loop improvement: rein in length/complexity on open-ended questions.

**Cross-check (blind Elo, text-only):** favoured B on Q_ERGO+Q2, L on Q3 — tracks the CS-panel view (arms ~tied), NOT the expert-inclusive combined view. Same lesson: automated signals under-detect the loop gain the domain expert sees.

### LB-095 addendum | 2026-07-12 15:55 CEST | [CS] | judge parse-repair (reasoning dim) before final blind scorecard

First full batch scored all 9 but **8/9 came back with `reasoning=None`** (R1 was fine — scored earlier under the interactive path). Root cause (reproduced live, not guessed): `claude-sonnet-5` interpreted the rubric key **`reasoning`** as "give your reasoning" and emitted PROSE there (dropping the `reasoning_reason` twin), so the aggregator's `isinstance(int,float)` filter correctly discarded it → None. The other 4 dims (grounding/completeness/usefulness/creativity) returned integers correctly. **Fair fix (no rubric/anchor/criterion change):** appended a STRICT OUTPUT CONTRACT coda to the judge prompt forcing each of the 5 dims to be an INTEGER 1–5 with justifications only in the `*_reason` twins; committed harness (`judge.py`) untouched — the coda lives on the adapter instance's `make_judge_fn`. Validated: all 3 personas now return integer `reasoning` on R2. First-batch scores archived to `blind_scores_v1_reasoning_none/` for provenance; re-scoring all 9 with the fixed judge. (First-batch composites, reasoning-missing, for the record: R1 2.64, R2 2.16, R3 3.32, R4 2.52, R5 2.20, R6 2.37, R7 2.17, R8 2.70, R9 2.49 — these will shift once the reasoning dimension is populated.)

## LB-098 | 2026-07-12 CEST | [CS] | BUG FOUND during Step-3 QC: the format coda silently zeroed the CREATIVITY gate for all 9 (same class as the LB-095 reasoning-dim bug); fix + surgical re-score (resolution appended below)

**Found in QC before writing BLIND_ANALYSIS (this is exactly the "validate before trusting a dimension" discipline).** In the completed Opus batch, the **creativity dimension came back flat 1.0 for all 9 answers**, with `plausibility_gate=0.0` AND `reasoning_trace_gate=0.0` AND `hallucination_flag=true` for every one — implausible as a real signal (9 independent answers cannot all have literally zero plausibility and zero reasoning trace). The 4 other dims discriminate normally (grounding 1–3, reasoning 4–4.7, completeness 4.7–5, usefulness 3.3–4.3).

**Root cause (reproduced live, not guessed).** The driver appends `_FORMAT_CODA` to EVERY `host.llm` judge call. That coda tells the model to return the FIVE RUBRIC dims (grounding/reasoning/completeness/usefulness/creativity) as integers — but the **creativity panel** (`run_creativity_panel`, `_CREATIVITY_SYSTEM`) has a DIFFERENT schema: it must return `plausibility` + `reasoning_trace` (1–5) + `redflags` + `reasoning_chain_quote`. Re-running one creativity call with the coda live confirmed the model emitted `{grounding:5, reasoning:5, completeness:4, usefulness:4, creativity:4, …}` — the rubric schema — and NOT `plausibility`/`reasoning_trace`. So `run_creativity_panel._agg("plausibility")=None`, `_agg("reasoning_trace")=None` → `gate(None)=0.0` → `creativity_index = novelty × 0 × 0 = 0` → creativity dim floored to 1.0 for all 9. Same failure class as LB-095 (a judge reading a key name as an instruction / wrong schema imposed), now in the creativity panel; the LB-095 parse-gate missed it because that gate only checks the 5 rubric dims, not the 2 creativity-panel keys. (exp-001 was unaffected — it predates the coda; its creativity dim discriminated 1.49–2.30.)

**Fix (format-only, fair, Opus-only preserved).** (1) Panel-aware coda in `run_opus_scoring.py`'s `OpusAdapters.make_judge_fn`: when `system == _CREATIVITY_SYSTEM` (exact match — the harness passes that literal), append a CREATIVITY-specific coda forcing `plausibility` + `reasoning_trace` to INTEGER 1–5 with justifications in `*_reason` twins and redflags as a list; the rubric panel keeps `_FORMAT_CODA`. No rubric/anchor/criterion/model change; still `claude-opus-4-8` everywhere. (2) Parse-gate extended to also require numeric `plausibility` + `reasoning_trace` from the creativity panel, so this can never silently pass again. (3) Surgical re-score: the 4 rubric dims + novelty (deterministic) + citation verification are provably INDEPENDENT of the creativity-panel schema bug and were computed correctly, so re-running the full batch would only add sampling noise to valid numbers AND re-spend the expensive citation-entailment budget — dangerous given the prior frame died on the 2.0M ceiling. Instead I re-ran ONLY the creativity panel (9×2 raters = 18 Opus calls) with the fixed coda, recomputed `creativity_index` + `weighted_composite` via the harness's OWN `composite.py` functions (not hand arithmetic), and rewrote the 9 rows + scorecards with a `_creativity_refix` provenance marker. RESOLUTION (corrected composites + per-answer plausibility/reasoning_trace) appended below.

### LB-098 RESOLUTION | 2026-07-12 CEST | [CS] | creativity re-score DONE (the fix code + 18-call re-run actually executed here)

The fix code was written AFTER the LB-098 discovery note above (panel-aware `_CREATIVITY_CODA` + exact-match router in `make_judge_fn` + parse-gate extended to require numeric `plausibility`/`reasoning_trace`), driver recompiled clean. Then the surgical re-score ran: creativity panel re-called for all 9 (2 raters each = 18 Opus calls) with the fixed coda, `creativity_index` + `weighted_composite` recomputed via the harness `composite.py` functions (not hand arithmetic), 9 rows rewritten in `blind_scores_opus/` with a `_creativity_refix` provenance block; pre-fix rows preserved in `blind_scores_opus_pre_creativity_refix/` (DO-NOT-USE README). Validated first on R3 (plausibility=5, reasoning_trace=5 → creativity 3.6, hallucination_flag False) before the full run.

**Corrected creativity dim + composite (creativity was floored to 1.0 for all 9 pre-fix):**

All figures §9.1 bbox-clean + §9.2 perceptually checked (fig3 label/dot collision fixed). All artifacts saved with platform version IDs. **exp-002 COMPLETE.**

**Interpretation for the Metascience Project mission:** qualified YES — the **v8 agentic loop beats the raw baseline** (and the earlier v7 loop), consistently across an independent human expert + LLM panel, clearest on creativity/reasoning for concrete design tasks. v7 did NOT clear the bar → loop *design* matters, not mere presence; v7→v8 was the productive iteration. Boundary: open-ended conceptual Q2 → baseline won. Powered follow-up needs more questions + within-cell replication.


## LB-104 | 2026-07-13 19:09 CEST | [CS2] | exp-003 (FINAL, T-cell Perturb-seq) — BOTH arms delivered; results documented (blank-CS → IMPDH2/mycophenolic acid/asthma; v9-loop → PKM2/micheliolide/MS)

**What this logs.** exp-003, the final experiment, has RUN. Both arms' deliverables are in `experiments/exp-003_final-tcell-perturb/02_results/`. Operator asked CS2 to review + document (no scoring — see below). This entry records what was run, what each arm produced, and honest caveats. No science was re-verified by CS2; the claims below are the ARMS' delivered claims.

**Design that actually ran (locked with operator this session, CS2).** Category-3 translational data test. **2 arms: B = blank CS (safety-only guardrail) vs L9 = v9 loop.** Question (verbatim, byte-identical to both arms): *"Starting from this genome-scale CD4+ T-cell Perturb-seq dataset, identify a natural metabolite or nutraceutical that could be used to treat patients with an autoimmune disease of your choice. Present your results, methodology, scientific rationale, and an optimal pilot experiment to test your prediction."* Delivery decisions: **output = a single PDF, publication-style report** (replaced the presentation-folder format); **dataset = DOI-only pointer** (bioRxiv 2025.12.23.696273, Marson-lab genome-scale CD4+ T-cell Perturb-seq on CZI VCM) + an explicit **compute-caution note** ("dataset is very large, you run on a small laptop — do not download/load the raw data; work from a tractable subset / processed data"). Both notes were byte-identical to both arms → fairness backbone intact. Runs executed from the copy-paste START prompts (blank-CS guardrail + question; v9 bootstrap intake), not from the setup files (see OPEN ITEM).

**ARM B — blank CS (baseline).** Deliverables: `02_results/presentation CS blank T-cell perturb/` = `report.pdf` (621 KB) + `report.html` + 3 PNG figures (PDF/HTML only; no md/trace set). 
- **Answer:** IMPDH2 (rate-limiting enzyme of de novo guanine-nucleotide synthesis) → **mycophenolic acid** (a natural *Penicillium* metabolite; approved prodrug mycophenolate mofetil) → **type-2 / eosinophilic asthma**.
- **Method:** honoured the compute-caution — did NOT download raw (~1.8 TB); streamed only cytokine-readout columns of the 16.8 GB `GWCD4i.DE_stats.h5ad` via HDF5 partial reads (~30 MB working matrix, ~1 GB peak). Screened 11,526 knockdowns; IMPDH2 ranked 1st of 576 druggable metabolic enzymes for selective type-2 suppression (IL-4/5/13 down, Th1/Treg spared); pathway-coherence across de novo purine enzymes; validated sign convention with MEN1 positive control; matched the type-2 axis to asthma via Open Targets GWAS; cited an orthogonal human result (Powell 2001, MPA inhibits allergen-driven IL-5) as prior validation.
- **Rigour signals:** on-target QC, cross-donor r=0.82, limitations section (transcriptional not protein readouts; modest FDR on sparse cytokines; MPA is a fungal metabolite not a dietary nutraceutical — honest). ~10 unique external identifiers (PMIDs/DOIs/GEO/SRA).

**ARM L9 — v9 loop.** Deliverables: `02_results/presentation v9 loop T-cell perturb/` = `report.pdf` (1.05 MB) + full presentation set (`result.md`, `reasoning.md`, `sources.md`, `process_trace.json` [26-action, ACTION-labelled], `figures/` ×3).
- **Answer:** PKM2 (pyruvate kinase M2; nuclear dimer potentiates STAT3-driven effector program) → **micheliolide (MCL)**, a natural guaianolide sesquiterpene lactone (feverfew-derived, covalent PKM2-Cys424 tetramer-stabiliser; clinical prodrug DMAMCL/ACT001) → **multiple sclerosis**.
- **Method:** same compute-light access (read the DE tensor `GWCD4i.DE_stats.h5ad`, 33,983 perturbation-conditions × 10,282 genes, by HTTP byte-range; 8 measured cytokines). Two-axis effector-vs-activation selectivity screen (suppress GM-CSF/IFN-γ, spare IL-2); pre-specified scoring fixed before ranking; sign convention validated on TBX21/STAT3/LAT/LCP2/ZAP70; PKM nominated on a biology-then-tractability walk-down (11,526 usable → 195 rows passing significance+reproducibility → 143 post-confound → PKM).
- **Loop-machinery fingerprints visible in the report (the v9 upgrades doing their job):** explicit **belief-ledger** (DATASET / LITERATURE / INFERENCE, every non-trivial claim carries a PMID/DOI/accession); a **direction-of-effect Table 2** distinguishing 6 non-identical perturbation modalities (CRISPRi vs genetic deletion vs TEPP-46 vs MCL vs prodrug) instead of falsely equating them; a **current-landscape check** that surfaced a 2026 human MS study (PKM2 targeting curbs patient T-cell cytokines) and then narrowed its own novelty claim honestly to "genome-scale causal nomination + natural-product covalent chemotype"; a **decisive falsifiable pilot** (2×2 compound×CRISPRi epistasis, interaction as primary endpoint, off-target/isoform controls, feasibility costed); a 6-point limitations list including the honest null "no MS PKM-locus GWAS signal → functional not genetic nomination".

**CS2 observations (documentation, not scoring).**
- Both arms honoured the compute-caution and produced grounded, publication-style PDFs with a clear metabolite→autoimmune-disease→pilot chain — neither collapsed on the "very big dataset / small laptop" constraint. The DOI-only + caution prompt worked.
- Both figure sets are clean, publication-grade (checked fig1 of each visually): no label overlap, sensible palette, real axes/legends — no "AI-slop" symptoms. (The Gate-2 figure-quality add-on, LB-089/090, targets exactly this; blank-CS figures were also clean here, so exp-003 does not by itself isolate that add-on's effect.)
- **Divergence is the interesting result:** identical question + data → two different targets (IMPDH2 vs PKM2), two different diseases (eosinophilic asthma vs MS), two different natural products (mycophenolic acid vs micheliolide). Both defensible; the v9 report carries visibly more epistemic-hygiene scaffolding (belief-ledger, modality table, self-novelty-check, falsifiable-interaction pilot).

**Honest caveats / scope.**
1. **No scoring.** Operator ruling this session: exp-003 is a **showcase comparison** — both PDFs go to the hackathon judges to decide; no CS-side rubric/harness scoring, no two-key blind, no the operator rubric pass (that machinery was exp-002). So this entry documents deliverables, not a measured win.
2. **Not CS2-verified.** I did not re-run the analyses, re-verify the PMIDs/DOIs/accessions, or check the biology. Targets, effect sizes (e.g. IMPDH2 type-2 log2FC −4.5; PKM GM-CSF z=−3.66), and literature claims are as reported by each arm.
3. **n=1 per arm, single question** — a demonstration on one hard real-data problem, not a powered comparison.

**OPEN ITEM (flagged, not acted).** The exp-003 setup files still hold CS1's DRAFT skeleton — `01_setup/test-set/questions.json` (status DRAFT / run_flag NOT READY, text `<<PLACEHOLDER>>`) and `00_hypothesis.md` (`<<PENDING>>` arms/question). The runs used the locked prompts I handed the operator, so the folder's setup files do NOT yet reflect what actually ran (question, PDF output, DOI-only delivery, B-vs-L9 arms). Recommend filling them to match (CS2 draft → operator confirm → surgical write) so the experiment folder is self-documenting for the submission. Not done here — this entry is documentation only.

**Provenance.** Dataset DOI 10.64898/2025.12.23.696273 (URL-verified on bioRxiv this session; live public S3 bucket `s3://genome-scale-tcell-perturb-seq/` inspected — 12 cell-level h5ad 119–173 GB each, DE_stats.h5ad 16.8 GB, + author CSV supp tables). Both reports read in full this session; fig1 of each viewed. Latest prior LB = LB-103 [CS] (exp-002 complete). This is LB-104 [CS2], append-only.
